The Panchen Lama Arrived in Beijing Yesterday Afternoon

Paid Respects to Chairman Lin and Others in the Afternoon

Attended the Fourth Plenary Session This Morning

(Nanjing) The Panchen Lama arrived in Beijing at 1:00 PM on the 24th on a special train from Beiping, accompanied by Lin Xiang and Leng Rong, special commissioners for welcoming the Panchen Lama, as well as Liu Jiaju, a Khenpo (abbot), technicians, attendants, and others, totaling more than ten people. They brought wireless radio equipment, cars, and many pieces of luggage. Dai Chuanxian, Huang Musong, Shi Qingyang, Wang Yongbin, and Lu Chao, representative of Chairman Lin, He Yaozu, representative of Chairman Chiang, Chu Minyi, representative of President Wang, as well as all staff members of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission and the Panchen Lama Office, the National Government Civil Affairs Office, the Military Attache's Office, the Control Yuan, the Judicial Yuan, the Ministry of Justice, the Examination Yuan, the Examination Committee, Inner Mongolian representatives, Qinghai students in Beijing, and representatives of the people, totaling more than 2,000 people, came to the station to welcome him. Two police and security teams provided security. Staff members of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission were in charge of reception. When the special train arrived at the station, the band played music, and the police and security saluted. Dai, Chu, Huang, Shi, and others boarded the train and shook hands with the Grand Master, and each presented a Hada (ceremonial scarf). Then they got off the train together. The Panchen Lama, supported by his attendants, walked out of the station and boarded a ferry to cross the river. The Panchen Lama and Dai rode in the same car to the Panchen Lama's residence at No. 5 Shenjia Lane. Lin and Wang visited and left after a brief conversation. In the afternoon, the Panchen Lama paid respects to Lin, Wang, and Chiang. He attended the plenary session in the morning of the 25th. According to the Panchen Lama, who spoke to a Central News Agency reporter at his residence, he had been away from Beijing for more than a year. In the spring of last year, due to the North China Incident, he was ordered by the commander of the Beiping Military Branch to travel west to Xuanhua, and received telegrams from various leagues and banners welcoming him to preach the Dharma. Later, he preached the Dharma in Ujimqin and Xilingol League and other places, which took five years to complete. Afterwards, he was stationed at Bailing Temple. Recently, he was summoned to Beijing by President Wang via telegram to discuss border affairs and attend the plenary session. Also, due to the passing away of the Dalai Lama, Chairman Lin and President Dai, among others, established altars to offer prayers, and instructed him to preside over the ceremony, so he set out for Beijing. At the beginning of the Inner Mongolian autonomy issue, he immediately informed all the princes to respect the wishes of the Central Government. Later, Minister Huang came to the temple to meet with the princes, and he made every effort to mediate. The princes deeply understood the great righteousness, so the autonomy issue was resolved. All Mongolian banners have sent personnel to Beijing to thank the Central Government for its benevolence. As for the passing of the Dalai Lama, he only learned about it after receiving a telegram from Beijing. He was deeply saddened by the news. Although he and the Dalai Lama had some misunderstandings in the past, they have recently been cleared up. The Dalai Lama had expressed his welcome for him to return to Tibet. He was deeply saddened by his sudden death. In addition to ordering all the lama temples in Mongolia, Tibet, and Qinghai to chant sutras and offer prayers, he also wrote a book, instructing the Dalai Lama to reincarnate as soon as possible so that the political and religious leadership would have someone to preside over it. There are rumors that chaos has recently occurred in Tibet, but he has not heard of it yet. He has no suggestions for the plenary session. Whether he will enter Tibet or not is all up to the Central Government. He has just arrived in Beijing, and his future movements have not yet been decided. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 24th)

Commentary

Rescuing Northeastern Students Who Have Lost Their Education - A Caution

For the past two years, the Northeast Four Provinces have been in turmoil. The sudden outbreak of the Mukden Incident (September 18th Incident) ignited national righteous indignation, leading to a courageous fight against the tyrannical invaders. Countless people have sacrificed their lives under the enemy's swords and guns, and in the line of fire. While these heroic sacrifices may not be enough to recover the Northeast, they are enough to bring glory to the nation and add color to the history of the Northeast's fall. Recently, Northeastern youths, reflecting on the past, cannot suppress their indignation. Witnessing the invaders' unyielding ambitions to completely annex the Northeast, transforming the former Three Eastern Provinces into what Korea is today, their emotions of grief and anger are even stronger than those of youths in the interior. We anticipate that among the intellectuals from the Northeast Four Provinces, except for a few who have surrendered to Japanese imperialism, none do not long for the recovery of their homeland.

However, today's China is deeply ill. To break through the current difficulties, a period of stability is necessary. From this stability, a methodical construction can be planned, followed by adequate preparations. Consequently, many youths feel impatient and frustrated, believing that waiting for the Yellow River to clear is impossible. This is understandable, as the economic lives of youths originally from the Northeast were generally better before the September 18th Incident, due to the region's superior economic conditions compared to the interior.

Therefore, their personal living environments were also better. However, this unprecedented blow abruptly turned a once prosperous area into foreign territory overnight. Their means of livelihood were suddenly overturned, and their assets were even confiscated, leaving them with nowhere to return. They had no choice but to turn to Tianjin and Beiping, with a bleak future and no idea where to go. This situation is truly pitiable.

The total number of Northeastern students who have transferred to schools in Tianjin, Beiping, and other places is estimated to be around 10,000. The government has instructed all schools to exempt Northeastern students from tuition fees. Recently, a stipend plan has been drafted, both to encourage the diligent study of these afflicted youths and to provide relief to homeless students. This is indeed a measure to revitalize national consciousness. However, the total number of youths and children in the Northeast who are of education age is at least over 400,000. Now, under Japanese oppression, they are either unable to continue their education due to economic exploitation, unwilling to accept their slave-like education due to Japanese political coercion, restricted by their location, or forced by circumstances to languish under the iron heel of the Japanese army, suffering in silence for days on end. Their numbers are tens, if not hundreds, of times greater than the number of Northeastern students who have lost their education and drifted into the interior. While it is impossible to reach those youths under the Japanese army's iron heel, every effort should be made to provide immediate relief to the Northeastern students drifting in the interior, to prevent them from losing their education and to enable them to achieve something, so that they can serve the country in the future and shoulder the arduous task of national salvation. This is of utmost importance and cannot be ignored.

Furthermore, we have something else to say. While immediate relief should be provided to youths who have lost their education, those who have been displaced and lost their homes due to the resistance against Japan, with nowhere to go, should not be left unemployed and destitute for long, lest they add another layer of difficulty to the national movement in the future. Thinking of this, the number of unemployed people in our country today is vast, and many cannot be helped. It is not just the Northeastern refugees. However, Northeastern refugees have suffered the most and been the most severely afflicted. Therefore, while providing relief to Northeastern students, policies should also be quickly implemented to aid Northeastern refugees. Whether by establishing public works projects or promoting industries specific to the Northeastern people, efforts must be made to ensure that all unemployed people have work, whether in agriculture, industry, intellectual labor, or commercial transport. They must all be integrated into the production process, which will undoubtedly contribute to China's future revival.

News from Moscow

Kashgar in Southwestern Xinjiang Declares Independence

Headsman of Khotan Takes Initiative

Openly Establishes Government

Engages in Collusion with Afghanistan and India

(Moscow) According to the TASS news agency in Tashkent, a new government has been established in Kashgar, supported by the Hui headsman of Khotan. The new government has declared that the entire western part of Xinjiang is under its jurisdiction and has announced its secession from China. It is reported that a merchant named Dumora has been appointed as the chief representative of the new government and has led a delegation to Afghanistan to negotiate a treaty of friendship. The delegation also plans to visit India. The new government has issued a declaration expressing its independence and has called for the expulsion of Chinese people from Xinjiang. (23rd Reuters Telegram)

(Moscow) According to reports from Tashkent, Kashgar (Shule), the largest center in southern Xinjiang, has established a new government, supported by the Hui headsman of Khotan, whose territory is close to the border of British India (Kashmir). The head of the new government is a merchant named Sabit Damulla, who is a subordinate of the headsman. The new government claims its territory as the entire western section of the new province, declaring its secession from China and safeguarding its independence. It has also dispatched a delegation to Afghanistan, which borders the southern part of the new province, to negotiate mutual recognition with the Afghan government in Kabul. According to reports from Kabul, the delegation also plans to visit India. Sabit Damulla is inviting Turks who are exiled in India and Japan, who harbor anti-Kemalist sentiments, to train troops. Kashgar has already announced the new government's declaration of independence, with the slogan "Expel the Han Chinese from Xinjiang." (24th TASS Telegram)

The Ma army in Ningxia is doing its best to resist. The authorities here are very dissatisfied with Sun's defiance of orders to advance west. After requesting instructions from the Central Government on how to handle the situation, they will take action. Hou Cheng, who was ordered to go to Shanxi, has temporarily stayed in Taiyuan, and it is uncertain when he will return to Beiping. (24th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Beiping) Song Zheyuan is scheduled to leave Beiping for Zhangjiakou on the 26th. Qin Decun will accompany him. The situation in Ningxia is extremely urgent. It is reported that Song is trying to mediate. The authorities in North China are still awaiting orders from the Central Government on how to handle the situation before instructing both sides to comply. A telegram from Ningxia on the 22nd reported that the Gansu and Qinghai armies are on standby to advance. (24th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Sun Dianying's telegram, urgently addressed to the Fourth Plenary Session of the Kuomintang Central Committee, the Central Executive Committee, the Executive Yuan, the Legislative Yuan, the Judicial Yuan, the Control Yuan, and the Examination Yuan: I, a simple military man, lack learning. After the War of Resistance against Japan, the Central Government, mindful of the hard-fought lives of tens of thousands of officers and soldiers, ordered us to go to Qinghai to reclaim wasteland. Previously, Chairman Ma of Ningxia did not allow us to pass through. Recently, due to the extreme cold and snowy weather in the Wulin area, with no housing and exposed to the elements, frostbite and deaths are inevitable. After consulting with Director Yan, he agreed to allow my army to be stationed in a part of the fertile land in the southwest of Suiyuan Province to spend the winter, not to march the entire army. Chairman Ma still misunderstands, stopping the troops advancing on the road to Shizuizi. After receiving orders, I immediately ordered the troops to stop advancing. However, the troops advancing through the Hedong area had not yet reached Wulin when the Ningxia Ma army, claiming that Wulin was under Ningxia's jurisdiction, sent troops to counterattack and wiped out my battalion under Li, resulting in a conflict. (Omitted) I earnestly request the speedy dispatch of senior officials to investigate the facts, clearly order punishment, and also request that these tens of thousands of stranded and impoverished officers and soldiers be graciously dealt with. Although we are stranded in the wilderness, with limited options, lacking food and clothing, crying out in hunger and cold, with nowhere to return, we dare not disobey your orders, and will do our utmost with our foolish sincerity, and repay the country's gracious kindness with our hot blood and heads. I humbly submit my request for your consideration. Qinghai Reclamation Director and Commander of the 41st Army Sun Kuiyuan respectfully bows. (24th Dispatch) (Beiping) Ligangbao, only thirteen miles from Ningxia's provincial capital, has been occupied by Sun Dianying's army. It is feared that the provincial army defending Pingluo will have to surrender because their retreat route has been cut off. The situation in Ningxia's provincial capital is very serious, and communication with Beiping may have been interrupted. (24th Reuters Telegram)

Central Propaganda Committee's Message to the People of the Nation

To Quell the Fujian Rebellion

Aiming to Unify Will

(Nanjing) The Central Propaganda Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang's message to the people of the nation regarding quelling the Fujian rebellion reads as follows: Since the rebel Chen Mingshu and others colluded with bandits and launched a rebellion, raising troops in Fujian, the news of the turmoil spread far and wide, arousing indignation throughout the country. Denouncing their crimes and demanding their punishment, the righteous cause was awe-inspiring. The Central Government, concerned about Fujian, was determined to safeguard the foundation of the nation, and thus ordered the army to swiftly suppress and eliminate them. The power of the military forced the rebel army to collapse and flee, and the fundamental suppression is imminent. This is due to the strategic command of the military leaders, the loyalty and courage of the soldiers at the front, and the support of public opinion and the condemnation of the people, which clearly distinguished right from wrong. Now, after quelling the rebellion, the Central Government, deeply concerned about the people's suffering, hereby proclaims several points to our people: The Three Principles of the People of our Party are the highest principles led by our Party Leader to revive the Chinese nation and lead the national revolution. Although they have not been fully realized due to internal and external troubles, each rebellion has made the principles more evident. All heresies and fallacies cannot shake them in the slightest. As of today, our Party's principles are intertwined with national construction and national survival, and cannot be separated. Those who betray our Party's principles and undermine the national revolution are tantamount to destroying national construction and endangering national survival. They will inevitably be subjected to the sanctions of public justice of the entire nation, and will hardly be spared, and their downfall will follow. Moreover, under the leadership of our Party Leader, we have engaged in the national revolution, undergoing decades of struggle and countless failures before overthrowing the Qing Dynasty and establishing the Republic of China. In 1926, we launched the Northern Expedition, continuing the heroic struggle and sacrifice, in order to eliminate the warlords and revive the Republic of China. Therefore, our Party bears the mission of nurturing, safeguarding, constructing, and prospering the Republic of China, ensuring that the country enters the realm of freedom and equality, and that the people advance towards happiness and prosperity, so that the national revolution will be completely successful and the Three Principles of the People will be fully realized, and only then will we not betray our Party's mission. Those who endanger the unity and peace of the people and undermine the revival and construction of the Republic of China will be exterminated by our Party with all our strength. However, social trends, if not governed, will lead to chaos. Once the vital energy is full, external evils will naturally subside. Learning from past events, we know that to transform chaos into order, the fundamental key lies in the Republic of China's ability to defend and govern itself, and its spirit of striving for survival. Therefore, strengthening social organization is extremely important. If social organization is sound, the people's strength will naturally be strong, which can curb the spread of heresies and sanction the occurrence of rebellions. The outbreak of the Fujian rebellion was extremely rampant, but it was gradually quelled in less than two months. This is not only due to the appropriate military mobilization, but also to the public's condemnation. This shows that the soundness of social organization is closely related to the elimination of rebellions. Furthermore, we would like to say something to the youth of the nation: Domestic reactionaries often try to exploit young people, deceiving them with heresies and fallacies, and enticing them with empty fame and meager profits. Some young people, due to their weak knowledge and wavering will, often disregard right and wrong and willingly become tools. Young people are the pillars of future society and the backbone of national construction. Their mission is extremely important. However, those who have lost their minds and love chaos, in order to achieve their manipulative purposes, do not hesitate to lead them astray, trapping them in punishment, damaging the vital energy of society, and destroying the vitality of the nation. This is especially heartbreaking. In this Fujian rebellion, the rebels arbitrarily exploited young people, using them as tools and making them their sacrifices, which is truly the height of depravity. Young people, reflecting on the past, should also be keenly aware, act cautiously, and encourage each other, channeling their thoughts into the right track and cultivating a solid foundation of knowledge, in order to shoulder the mission of the nation's future. The above points should be deeply understood and jointly corrected by all our people after the incident, in order to curb the seeds of danger and move towards the path of construction. Today, with internal and external troubles, the foundation of the nation is precarious. Only by uniting the will and ability of the people of the nation, with everyone working together, can we maintain the life of the nation and glorify the spirit of history. All our people must unify their will, concentrate their talents, and develop their spirit, in order to turn chaos into order and strive diligently. The saying "difficult times build the nation" is a clear lesson from the past. The historical examples of striving for strength and wiping out humiliation are clear. Therefore, we have listed the key points for everyone to encourage each other. (24th Central News Agency Telegram)

Direct Franco-German Negotiations Fail, Prospects for Disarmament Dim Further

British Cabinet Meeting Leans Towards Further Mediation

If There Is Still No Breakthrough, a Convention to Maintain the Status Quo Will Be Agreed Upon

(Paris) The situation on disarmament has become dark again. Reuters has learned from reliable sources in Paris that the French government is disappointed with the German reply. The attitude expressed by Germany in its reply is described by the French as delaying and unfavorable to bilateral negotiations. Therefore, from now on, all hopes for disarmament will gradually fade. The exchange of notes between France and Germany only shows that the two sides have major differences of opinion in principle. It is said that the German reply did not make any concessions to the French proposal, but only offered theoretical arguments in a polite way to prove the legitimacy of its previous demands. The note also raised many technical questions, which are currently being carefully studied by the ministers of the French defense departments. The French government is paying close attention to tomorrow's British Cabinet meeting, which will discuss whether Britain should propose any suggestions to Germany to resolve the arms dispute. Germany also recently replied to Britain's inquiry about certain aspects of the equality demands, implying that Germany welcomes such suggestions. The main result of accepting this invitation will be for Britain to step in and mediate, and to make suggestions to alleviate the Franco-German conflict. However, France now feels that the executive committee of the Disarmament Conference should firmly decide at the London meeting in February whether the disarmament convention should be signed by Germany, so that the Disarmament Conference can decide its own future. The meaning of certain aspects is that countries should, in accordance with the suggestion of Czech Foreign Minister Dr. Benes, conclude a convention, mutually agreeing to maintain the current level of armaments without expanding them, and stipulating that if any party violates the convention, all signatory countries can withdraw from the convention and act freely. (23rd Reuters Telegram)

British Inclination to Mediate

Commercial Recovery Depends on Successful Disarmament

(London) The British Cabinet will convene tomorrow to consider Germany's response to France's disarmament proposals, as well as various questions concerning this matter from Britain. Germany has requested Britain to act as a third-party mediator. The British Cabinet finds this to be a difficult decision. At the same time, public opinion in London tends to oppose involvement in the Franco-German affair. However, leading politicians believe that the recovery of world commerce depends on the success of disarmament. Therefore, it is believed that Britain's acceptance of Germany's request could lead to an earlier successful disarmament. (Reuters, 23rd)

(London) The Cabinet's Disarmament Subcommittee met this afternoon, chaired by Lord President of the Council Baldwin, as Prime Minister MacDonald had gone to the Leeds area to continue campaigning for the National Government's policies. During the meeting, Foreign Secretary Simon explained to his colleagues the German reply to France and the answers to the points raised by British Ambassador to Germany, Sir Eric Phipps, on December 20th.

According to well-informed sources, the Cabinet seems to advocate Britain acting as a mediator again. While the mediation approach will not deviate from Prime Minister MacDonald's original disarmament plan, recent German negotiations will be taken into account to achieve mutual adaptation. Semi-official sources believe that Britain wants to "bridge" and connect the views of France and Germany. The Cabinet's Disarmament Subcommittee today is seeking a way to build this bridge. Although diplomatic circles are keeping this matter strictly confidential, the impression among those close to the government is more optimistic than yesterday. After studying the German reply, the government feels that although an immediate compromise is not possible, there is at least the possibility of reopening negotiations to seek a compromise. It is generally believed that the outcome of Britain's re-mediation will depend on the extent of concessions we can demand from both sides. This point is not concealed. (Havas, 23rd)

Truth about German Armaments

Will Make Demands with Strength in the Future

(London) A correspondent for The Times in Berlin has written a lengthy article examining German military activities under the rule of the National Socialist Party. His conclusion is that German rearmament is a fait accompli, or at least well on its way to completion. Since German rearmament cannot be eradicated at the root, the goal of European countries should be to compel Germany to rearm for peaceful purposes. The article states that Germany is deliberately moving towards military equality and pursuing this goal through rearmament. Germany's initial proposal to France involved a substantial increase in the German army. In the eighteen months since former Chancellor Papen took office, Germany has decided to rearm, as the nation's youth look forward to rearmament as a means of advancement, and industry expects rearmament to increase its orders. All kinds of desires rely on rearmament for satisfaction. Leading figures in German political circles have made declarations expressing their unwavering determination to rearm Germany immediately, without further delay. If Germany is prepared to negotiate with other countries, the negotiations will only concern the length of military service and the quantity of future Party army armaments. Therefore, German rearmament is no longer in question. The question is whether Germany is rearming because its national defense is not secure or whether it intends to use force to achieve its ultimate political goals. The correspondent then provides a detailed analysis of military technology, concluding that today we cannot ignore the irrefutable evidence. From now on, Germany will rely on its powerful military force to make demands. If we do not want to bury our heads in the sand and ignore the obvious facts, then it is almost inevitable that we will reach a satisfactory agreement with Germany on the issue of armaments. This is the only way to study whether Germany can cooperate sincerely to maintain peace in Europe. (Havas, 24th)

U.S. Senate Silver Committee Passes Roosevelt Currency Bill

But With Significant Amendments

Stabilization Fund Operation Limited to Two Years

(Washington) The currency bill proposed by President Roosevelt has been passed by the Senate Banking Committee by a majority of 15 votes to 2 votes, but with two amendments attached. The first stipulates that the Exchange Equalization Fund should be managed by a separate committee of five members: the Secretary of the Treasury, the Chairman of the Federal Reserve Bank, the Comptroller of the Currency, and two others appointed by the President. The second amendment limits the existence of the Exchange Equalization Fund to two years in theory but authorizes the President to extend the term if necessary. There are general concerns that currency may not be redeemable, and many advocate that the new dollar should be redeemable for large gold bars, according to the current French system. There are also deep concerns that credit expansion will be virtually unlimited after the bill is passed, which may lead to a sharp rise in prices and trigger another financial panic. The White House is also aware of this danger, so Roosevelt has indicated that the Civil Works Administration's funding, which was previously used to employ four million workers, will be halted on May 1st. (Havas, 23rd)

British Manchester Rejects Japanese Goods Movement

British Far East Navy to Centralize at Singapore

Secret Meeting on HMS Kent

The Mystery of European War Hero Allenby's Visit

(London) The news that British General Allenby, who enjoyed fame in the European War, is about to visit the Far East has led to speculation in Singapore and other places that General Allenby will participate in a British Far East naval conference. Although Allenby claims that his visit to the East is purely for leisure, he has ultimately failed to dispel rumors of his participation in the meeting. Therefore, the Admiralty and War Office have had to issue denials, stating that General Allenby is visiting the Far East in a purely private capacity, without any official mission, and that General Allenby is not currently an active member of the military.

Reuters learned from reliable sources that newspaper speculation related to the Singapore naval conference and defense projects is largely exaggerated. According to official statements, the Singapore conference is merely a routine event that occurs automatically, and the defense projects are simply being carried out in accordance with policies that were approved many years ago. Cabinet members have repeatedly stated this in the House of Commons, and there are no new developments or changes to the original purely local defense policy.

This statement is very different from various rumors. The source of newspaper speculation is likely due to the secret holding of the Singapore naval conference, which was held on the British ship Kent, which was docked in the most secluded location in the port of Singapore. This is why rumors have arisen.

It is heard that the agenda has the following four items: (1) Discussion of Singapore's future as a naval concentration point; (2) Progress of various naval base projects; (3) The situation in the Far East; (4) General events related to the local fleet. However, the Admiralty has not announced the agenda, so it is not yet fully known whether the above four items are accurate.

The Singapore conference began in 1921, but the current one is the first in the past eight years. Attendees include Vice Admiral Dreyer, Commander-in-Chief of the British Fleet in China; Vice Admiral Nasmith; Rear Admiral Dalgleish; Rear Admiral Watson; Governor of the Straits Settlements Clementi; and Commander of Malaya Sir Cecil Clementi, among others. (Reuters, 23rd)

(London) The Daily Mail today carried an editorial stating that the attention aroused by the Singapore naval conference proves that the policy issues of the British Empire in the Far East and the Pacific are becoming increasingly important. It also said that the situation created by the active naval policies of the United States and Japan may not necessarily harm the interests of the British Empire, but it is quite clear that the time has come for prudent consideration of the necessities of Singapore's defense. (Reuters, 24th)

(London) The Evening Standard published an editorial commenting on the opening of the British naval conference in Singapore, stating that all parties advocate making good use of Singapore's new naval port and defending it. This conference is tantamount to approving this proposition. From the standpoint of the British Empire, the significance of this conference is very great. The newspaper then explained Singapore's defense plan, saying that Britain absolutely needs to station a navy in the Far East. The newspaper continued, "Anyone who points out the severity of the situation runs the risk of being ridiculed as preparing for war, but the need to protect the sea lanes that British commerce must pass through is unanimously recognized by enlightened people all over the world." The Singapore naval port is not a threat, and Japan has understood this. Did Japanese Foreign Minister Hirota not recently say in a speech that the two major naval powers of East and West are in the same position and that there is a possibility of mutual cooperation to maintain peace? This is exactly the attitude that Britain wants. In short, the Singapore naval port is beneficial to peace, not a preparation for war. (Havas, 23rd)

Seiyukai (Constitutional Association) Members Advocate Active Policy Towards China

Tokonami Declares Determination to Protect the Constitution

(Tokyo) Yesterday's speech by Tokonami Takejirō, advisor to the Seiyukai Party, in the Diet was highly regarded by all sectors. (3) The military has recently adopted a policy of secrecy, unwilling to let the people know all important issues. Does the military really believe that the army can wage war abroad without the support of the people?

Japan's Warmongering Arouses Antipathy in Various Countries

The Military Reins in on the Brink of Precipice and Plans to Crack Down

(Tokyo) The remarks of young officers in the Japanese military have been interpreted in the United States, Russia, and Italy as the Japanese military's intention to create a war. Publishing companies and magazine supplements are catering to current preferences for war propaganda, such as "Hi no De's" (Rising Sun) "Future Record of the Japanese-American War" and "Our Navy" being confiscated in the United States, and Commander-in-Chief Suetsugu's remarks published in "Modern" being blamed by the US Naval Command as articles inciting war, etc. All countries are paying close attention to the military's remarks, and the issue was raised in the Japanese Diet yesterday, demanding that the government crack down on publications that incite war. It is heard that the Ministry of the Army, mindful of the extremely dangerous atmosphere at home and abroad, is also planning to crack down on this kind of speech. (Hualian Telegram, 24th)

(Tokyo) The Tokyo Shimbun (Eastern News) states that US newspapers in San Francisco commented on Foreign Minister Hirota's speech, saying that Japan loves peace and the United States also seeks peace, but the Japanese publishing industry is colluding with the military, vigorously promoting war, especially against the United States. The Japanese government allows its publishing and news media to publish articles that intimidate the United States and undermine US military institutions, and serious crackdowns should be carried out on such writings. (Hualian Telegram, 24th)

(4) The military is vigorously suppressing the speech of the people, single-mindedly wanting the people to believe that there will be a war in 1936, and does not allow the people to ask why there will be a war, and whether there will really be a war. What is the military's intention? (5) The military issued a statement last year opposing the alienation of the military and the people. Is the military's true intention to suppress speech, or is there really such a fact? Army Minister Hayashi's answer was very simple. Navy Minister Osumi also said that it was inconvenient to answer with facts, and if facts were answered, it would have an impact on foreign countries, so he could open a secret meeting to explain. Because the Minseito Party was pressing hard, the military could no longer refuse, and agreed to hold two secret meetings to explain the military's position, which ended at 4:48 pm. (Hualian Telegram, 24th)

(Tokyo) Katō Masanosuke, a member of the upper house belonging to the Minseito Party, questioned this morning in the Diet on financial problems and military preparedness, criticizing the military for deliberately exaggerating war propaganda and inciting war. The main points of his speech were as follows: The world economy is in turmoil, and the finances of all countries are inadequate, as is Japan's own difficulty. The United Kingdom has balanced its budget after two years of effort. Does the Japanese Ministry of Finance intend to take the United Kingdom as an example? The military is vigorously promoting the crisis of 1935. What kind of facts does the military's so-called crisis refer to? At present, due to the military's propaganda, many people believe that there will be a war in 1935, which has led the financial world to take a negative attitude and dare not invest actively. Observing the internal affairs of the United States and Russia, if Japan does not challenge the two countries, there will be no war. Because the military is promoting war, the Ministry of Finance is sacrificing everything to expand useless military preparedness. During a period of progress, it is not necessary to adopt a policy of contraction of finances, but comparing the budgets of the 8th and 9th years, next year's budget has exceeded 2.3 billion yuan. Does the government intend to increase taxes? Will the government still allow the Bank of Japan to buy up government bonds? (Hualian Telegram, 24th)

Reactions of Public Opinion in Various Countries to Hirota's Diplomatic Speech

No Less Than Declaring an Asian Monroe Doctrine

Harboring Ambitions to Control China

(London) Japanese Foreign Minister Hirota's speech in the House of Peers has aroused two conflicting interpretations in the press here. One is that Japan intends to invade all of China, and the other is that Hirota's attitude shows that he is moderate and intends to approach Europe and the United States. Political figures, however, take a compromise between the two, saying that Hirota's intention seems to be to declare an Asian Monroe Doctrine, which in itself is not without arguments, but may be detrimental to the development of British interests in the Far East. Political figures believe that the meaning of Hirota's speech is only this, and not as much as what the "Daily People's Voice" and the "Times" have said, the former saying that Japan has ambitions to control all of China, and the latter saying that Japan will cooperate with Europe and the United States, both of which are going to extremes. (Havas, 23rd)

Japanese-Russian Relations Becoming Increasingly Tense, Japan Feels Threatened by the United States and Russia Joining Hands

(Paris) There has been little commentary in France on the resignation of Japanese Army Minister Araki, due to the lack of sufficient information here on the relationship of Araki's resignation to its impact on Japanese foreign policy. However, people in general are very satisfied with the following: Although Japanese-Russian relations have always been tense, it seems that a conflict is not necessarily inevitable. Recently, Soviet Russian Heavy Industry Representative Kaganovich delivered a speech that truly expressed the Soviet Russian side's major concerns, but people in general believe that the restoration of normal relations between the United States and Russia is nothing less than a tranquilizing agent for the tense situation between Japan and Russia, and is truly a factor of stability in the Pacific. (Kaganovich is the secretary of the Central Committee of the Communist Party and the Moscow District Committee). (Havas, 23rd)

Various Countries Are Busy Preparing Policies Towards Japan; Empty Words of Peace Will Not Achieve Results

(Berlin) The Berliner Börsen-Zeitung commented on the Japanese Foreign Minister's speech in the House of Peers, considering it a masterpiece of a great statesman. It stated, "From Hirota's speech, it can be seen that Japan attaches great importance to the situation in China and its relations with Russia. Japan is closely observing the activities of Soviet Russia in China and reserves the possibility of intervention. Hirota clearly stated that the progress of diplomatic relations between Japan and Soviet Russia depends entirely on the attitude of Soviet Russia towards 'Manchukuo.' Foreign Minister Hirota repeatedly spoke of Japan's peaceful efforts in the Pacific, but he did not conceal the fact that Japan's national power development is sufficient to cause some danger." The newspaper concluded, "The U.S. Congress has already proposed a naval construction plan, and naval commanders from Britain, New Zealand, Australia, and other places are holding an Imperial Naval Conference in Singapore. Furthermore, the Central Committee of the Soviet Communist Party and Moscow Regional Secretary Kaganovich have also delivered speeches on international policy at the Moscow city district party congress. Therefore, the places where international conflicts may occur and the nature of the conflicts can be generally imagined." (Havas Dispatch, 23rd)

(Nanjing) The Central Machine Factory is being prepared with funds borrowed from the British Boxer Indemnity. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek Restricts the Purchase of Materials by Military Organizations

(Nanjing) Chairman Chiang Kai-shek stated that in the past, various military organizations have generally estimated and requested funds when ordering materials from abroad. There was no detailed plan beforehand, and no serious acceptance inspection was conducted afterward. The waste and extravagance involved were self-evident. Yesterday, he ordered the Ministry of Military Affairs to inform all subordinate units that in the future, if any military organization orders goods from abroad with a value of over 3,000 yuan, it must first submit its purpose and order plan, along with the necessary estimate, drawings, and samples. After the review and approval of the responsible auditing office, Chiang himself will personally approve it before a contract can be signed. When the goods are delivered, the auditing office must also be requested to inspect and audit them before the procedures can be completed. This will be a standing rule from now on and must not be deliberately violated. (Special Dispatch, 24th)

Banknotes Dance From a High Building

A Wealthy Greek Man Abhors Money

Passersby Scramble, Order Is Greatly Disrupted

Athens A wealthy Greek industrialist named Ramas developed a strange habit today. From the top of his residential building, he scattered banknotes of 100, 500, and 1,000 drachmas (the Greek currency) downwards, causing passersby to scramble for them. This news spread rapidly throughout the city, and tens of thousands of people gathered spontaneously, vying to grab the banknotes fluttering in the air. By the time the police arrived to suppress the situation, the scramble had turned into a riot. They had to mobilize reserve soldiers to disperse the crowd. The police then entered Ramas's residence and prohibited him from throwing banknotes again. However, when Lai saw the police enter his room, he tore up the piles of banknotes in front of him and told the police that he deeply hated this filthy money and was tired of being burdened by it. Later, the police, believing that he was mentally disturbed, sent him to a hospital. His family checked his accounts and found that he had scattered over 100,000 drachmas in a short period. (National News Agency Dispatch, 23rd)

Japan's Preparations for Disarmament (Tokyo Correspondence)

Convening a Joint Consultative Conference of the Three Ministries of Foreign Affairs, Army, and Navy

Three Principles for Dealing with Disarmament Have Been Decided

It will be two full years since Japan announced its withdrawal from the League of Nations in March of last year. Judging from Japan's political situation and military actions in the past year,

There is, of course, no hope of returning to the League of Nations before March of next year. However, in just over a year, Japan will formally withdraw from the League of Nations. Consequently, three major problems have arisen:

(1) The issue of returning the mandated territory of the South Pacific Islands.

(2) The issue of "Manchukuo" not being recognized by countries around the world.

(3) The issue of reducing naval armaments.

The leaders of the Japanese military and the government have decided to forcefully occupy the first issue and will never return it to the League of Nations. Because Japan already has considerable military facilities on the Caroline and Mariana Islands, it has made military preparations against the United States and Britain. Therefore, it will absolutely not readily relinquish control of the South Pacific Islands, either now or in the future. Regarding the situation in the puppet state, even within Japan, apart from the military authorities, there is some sense of alienation. However, only Japanese militarists claim it is a country, while all countries around the world have unanimously rejected Japan since the summer of last year. Although the reasons for this rejection should all be attributed to economic factors, politically, it cannot be denied that it is the result of Japan's encouragement of Puyi to create a puppet regime. The United States has stated its opposition, and Britain has also promoted anti-Japanese sentiment. It is feared that the current situation cannot be allowed to continue indefinitely, allowing Japan to act rampantly in East Asia.

Although optimists in Japanese military circles believe that the US fleet in the Pacific (including the Atlantic fleet) will return to the Atlantic together in April of this year, indicating a considerable understanding of Japan's position and expressing goodwill towards Japan. Therefore, Hirota's new diplomatic policy is particularly friendly to the United States. He believes that there is very little direct military conflict between Japan and the United States, and the current crisis has a high possibility of being averted. However, the reality is not so. The US fleet will still return to the Pacific this autumn. Although the presence of this fleet in the Pacific does not necessarily serve as a challenge, it is undoubtedly a threat to Japan. If Japan continues to proceed in this way, the crisis between Japan and the United States will continue to accumulate, and ultimately, there will only be war. At present, the United States certainly cannot adopt an offensive stance because the United States' naval strength does not have the certainty of victory. However, the United States has concentrated its Atlantic fleet in the Pacific, while refurbishing its unusable warships, and expanding its air force. Long-distance flights between San Francisco and Hawaii are also a trial with great military significance. Furthermore, it will build new warships according to the number allowed by the London Treaty.

Japan's attention to these factual changes will certainly not be relaxed. In addition to actively responding to the second naval replenishment plan, it has also made diplomatic preparations, especially in preparation for the Second Naval Conference. Japan's preparations for international armament issues are roughly as follows:

(1) The Director of the European and American Affairs Bureau of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs will convene a joint consultative conference of those related to the Army and Navy, which will meet once a week to study new issues arising in Europe and the United States. At the same time, the section chiefs of the Ministries of Foreign Affairs, Army, and Navy, and officials with the rank of colonel or above, will form a disarmament investigation and research committee to conduct specialized research on disarmament. The committee will collect all information on disarmament and formulate countermeasures to other countries.

(2) The ministers, vice ministers, and related bureau chiefs of the Ministries of Foreign Affairs, Army, and Navy will form a three-ministry disarmament executive committee. They believe that the invitation to the disarmament conference will be issued by Britain or the United States in June 1935, so Japan must complete all its preparations by October of this year at the latest.

As for Japan's principles on disarmament, first, it promotes an autonomous stance, not subject to any constraints, and demands equality in naval armaments, completely overturning the ratio stipulated by the Washington Treaty. Second, regarding the scope of the agenda, Japan advocates limiting it to naval-related issues such as "naval holdings," "coastal defenses," and "naval bases," and absolutely opposes involving other political issues. In other words, the Washington Nine-Power Treaty cannot be re-raised. Third, if countries have preparatory meetings on disarmament, Japan must participate; otherwise, it will refuse to attend the main conference. This is a countermeasure by Japan to the 1936 crisis and can also be seen as a glimpse of Japan's so-called national policy. (January 18, 1934, Tokyo)

The Situation in North China After the Declaration of Reform by the Puppet Organization

Japanese Troops Continue to Provoke

Traitors Active Everywhere

Beiping Correspondence: The puppet organization declared its reform on the 20th of this month. The puppet Pu Yi is scheduled to ascend the puppet throne on March 1st. It is reported that the Japanese aims are, firstly, to use Pu Yi's ascension to the throne to buy the hearts of the people in Manchuria and Mongolia; and secondly, to advance towards Chahar and Suiyuan to complete their Manchuria-Mongolia policy. As for North China, they will decide their strategy of invasion based on how we respond. After the Japanese and puppet troops in Eastern Chahar harassed Longmensuo, they temporarily withdrew their troops after our negotiations. However, they are still using the excuse that troops cannot be stationed along the Great Wall line to demand that we withdraw our troops stationed in the Longmensuo area. We argue that the Longmensuo area is not within the scope of the Tanggu Truce and it is impossible to withdraw our troops. The Japanese troops still disagree. Nishio Giichi, the commander of the 8th Division of the Japanese Army, sent a telegram to Shibayama, the military attaché of the Japanese Embassy, yesterday (the 22nd), pointing out that we had increased troops in Longmensuo and other places. Shibayama then visited He Yingqin and Huang Fu based on the telegram and verbally questioned them. He and Huang both stated that there was no such thing. Furthermore, at 2 PM yesterday, Qin Dechun visited Shibayama and formally replied, firmly denying the increase in troops, and asked Shibayama to forward the telegram to Nishio Giichi. This kind of action by the Japanese side is purely a provocation, regardless of whether the facts are true or not. Song Zheyuan, the Chairman of Chahar, who was visiting relatives in Tianjin, was summoned back to Beiping late last night. Today, he separately visited He and Huang. At the regular meeting of the Military Affairs Commission tomorrow (the 24th), the issue of Eastern Chahar will be brought up for discussion. After Song attends the meeting, he will immediately return to Chahar.

Recently, puppet rebels and traitors have been active in the Beiping and Tianjin areas, plotting wrongdoing. However, they have not succeeded due to the strict prevention by the authorities. Since the puppet organization announced its reform on the 20th, traitors have become even more arrogant. Recently, they have been sending threatening letters to various newspapers in Beiping and Tianjin in the names of the East Asia League, North China Residents, and the Yamato Club, etc., preventing the publication of anti-Japanese and critical writings on the puppet organization. The wording is extremely absurd. In addition to intensifying the prevention and arrest of the police and military police in Beiping and Tianjin, personnel have also been secretly dispatched to protect the newspaper offices to prevent unexpected events. (January 23rd)

The Situation in the Northwest is Increasingly Tense, with Fierce Fighting Between the Sun and Ma Factions

Sun's Troops Cross the River and Advance Westward, Besieging Pingluo

Gansu, Ningxia, and Qinghai Troops Mobilized to Defend Against Sun

Beiping Correspondence: Sun Dianying's troops' westward advance is reportedly due to the large number of soldiers and lack of supplies. They are trapped in Western Suiyuan and unable to survive, so they are heading west to find a way out. Sun was originally appointed as the Commissioner of Reclamation in the Qinghai Border Region. Reclamation and garrisoning in Qinghai would have been justified. However, due to circumstances and restrictions, the Northwest provinces will not allow Sun's troops to gain a foothold there. After a problem arose previously, the Central Government had no fundamental solution. It simply issued an order to temporarily suspend the westward advance, stay in the original defense areas, spend the winter, and discuss the matter later. Now, Sun's troops, with tens of thousands of starving soldiers, are desperately seeking food. Therefore, despite knowing that it violates the Central Government's orders, they cannot openly advance westward. Instead, they claim to be dispersing to defend the fertile fields, secretly planning to move west. Before the launch, they claimed on the one hand that they could not survive the winter and were dispersing to defend the fertile fields, and on the other hand, they obtained the consent of Yan of Shanxi to act as backup. Since the start of the campaign, they have adopted a method of undeclared war, first occupying Zhenkou, where Ningxia and Suiyuan meet, and then probing Shizuishan, the gateway to Ningxia. Ma Hongkui's troops in Ningxia had long been prepared for Sun. The Shizuishan area is strategically located and easy to defend, with heavy troops stationed there. Sun's troops, seeing that Ma's troops were prepared when they attacked Shizuishan, stopped their westward advance after a brief contact and claimed that they were complying with the order to stop the westward advance, detour to Woye, and move south along the Yellow River, dividing their forces to invade Ningxia. Ningxia and Suiyuan are separated by a river. While Shizuishan is easy to defend but difficult to attack, there are many ferries elsewhere and the defense line is long, making it easy to cross the river secretly. In addition, it is now the dead of winter, and the river is dry and frozen, making it possible to cross the river anywhere. The danger of the Yellow River is practically zero. After Sun's troops bypassed Shizuishan, they crossed the river and advanced westward, one route attacking Pingluo, and the other using cavalry to raid Ligangbao between Pingluo and Ningxia, attempting to cut off the connection between Pingluo and Ningxia. Ligangbao is 40 miles from Pingluo and about 60 miles from Ningxia. Yu Shiming's cavalry of Sun's troops has raided the area ten times but failed. They are now focusing all their efforts on attacking Pingluo, hoping to occupy Pingluo and gain a base in Ningxia, before advancing on the provincial capital of Ningxia. Ma Hongkui's troops also consider the terrain of Pingluo to be important and are doing their best to defend it. In recent days, the fighting in that area has been extremely fierce. If Sun's troops continue to advance westward, the war is bound to escalate.

In recent days, both Sun and Ma have sent telegrams to Beiping, engaging in a war of words. The authorities in Beiping believe that although Sun's troops are under the Beiping Military Affairs Commission, geographically they belong to the two Pacification Zones of Gansu, Ningxia, Qinghai, and Taiyuan. Therefore, they cannot let this matter go. On the one hand, they telegraphed Sun, ordering him to stop his westward advance. On the other hand, they sent personnel to seek the opinions of Yan of Shanxi, and telegraphed the situation to the Central Government to request instructions, striving to first stop the conflict between the two sides, and then discuss a solution in the long term. It is reported that Shanxi does not have any particular fondness for Sun. However, it is impossible for Shanxi to cooperate with other parties to resolve the issue of Sun's troops. This time, Sun's westward advance is a matter of Shanxi adopting a send-off policy. As Sun's troops move, Wang Jingguo's troops will follow. Since the 19th year, most of the guest troops stationed in Shanxi and Suiyuan have been withdrawn. Currently, the only remaining troops are those of Sun Dianying. His voluntary westward advance is what Shanxi has been praying for. (January 23rd)

The Mutiny in Yutian Expands

The Evil Consequences of Reorganizing Bandit Troops

Shi Yousan Pulling Strings Behind the Scenes

Tianjin Correspondence: The mutiny of Hu Xie Wu's Security Corps in Yutian County, Northern Hebei, led by Zhang Futang, has occupied the Yayang Hongqiao area for a week now. This matter has recently shown signs of expansion, and due to certain background relationships, the provincial authorities are finding it difficult to deal with. The Hu Xie Wu Security Corps was originally formed by reorganizing Shi Yousan's rebel army. After the Tanggu Truce was established, Shi Yousan's responsibility of being driven by the Japanese puppets was over. The puppet troops under his command could not be properly placed, so the provincial authorities, together with Li Jichun's puppet troops, reorganized them into security corps, led by Zhao Lei, Li Zuozhou, and Hu Xie Wu. Zhang Futang, the brigade commander of Shi's troops, was incorporated into one of the battalions of Hu Xie Wu's division. Due to budgetary concerns, the provincial authorities limited the number of officers and soldiers in each battalion to no more than 1,000. Hu Xie Wu's recruitment in Yutian actually led to the inability to manage the situation, and his subordinates refused to be reorganized. Therefore, although he wanted to reorganize according to the number set by the province, it was impossible. For several months, the 700-800 officers and soldiers left over after the reorganization could not be properly dealt with. He repeatedly came to the province to ask for instructions. In order to maintain the original plan, the province refused to make any changes. It also issued 3,000 yuan twice to Hu for the dismissal of the remaining officers, but Hu, despite receiving the money, did not dare to do so due to difficulties. Recently, he even used the excuse of insufficient pay to extort money from the local area. Merchants have already contributed several times and are unable to bear the burden. They telegraphed the province, asking them to instruct the division not to extort any more money. Based on the situation, the province strictly ordered the division to reorganize according to the set number. At this point, the division was secretly instigated by Shi Yousan, who was residing in Tianjin, to defect to the puppet side and request to be incorporated into the East Asia League Army. So on January 14th, the mutiny occurred. Zhang Futang initially led a detachment of about 550 people to Yayang Hongqiao Town, 35 miles from Yutian. The town is a famous commercial center in Yutian, with a well-fortified stronghold. The rebel army immediately occupied the town, looting and plundering, raping women, and committing all kinds of crimes. They closed the four gates of the stronghold and guarded them with bandits, prohibiting entry and exit, and demanding that the Chamber of Commerce pay 50,000 yuan. The Chamber of Commerce was unable to raise the money, so the president was arrested and shot. Wealthy merchants and residents were kidnapped. The local militia did not dare to attack rashly because the merchants and residents had not escaped. The rebel army, knowing that the government troops were hesitant to attack, became even more rampant, occupying the town and refusing to leave. On the 18th, the security corps in the city also mutinied one after another. One part fled to Yayang Hongqiao and joined the first group of rebels, and the other part occupied Hongqiao Town, 13 miles from the city, broke into the town, seized the militia's weapons, and shot more than 40 residents. Then, they looted for three days, and sent out a detachment to loot Lin Nan Cang Town, extorting 15,000 yuan from the Chamber of Commerce. Dong Tianhua, the magistrate of Yutian County, borrowed more than 3,000 militiamen from the nearby Zunhua, Fengrun, and Jixian counties on the 19th, surrounding Yayang Hongqiao and Hongqiao Town to eliminate the rebels. Zhang Futang led the rebel army to resist the attack, and set fire to the entire town of Yayang Hongqiao. The fire started on the night of the 20th, and was still burning on the evening of the 21st. Looking out into the night, the red light illuminated the sky, and the rebels were still resisting. The provincial government received a report a few days ago, and in addition to telegraphing the security corps in the war zone to suppress the rebellion, they also sent Yin Rugeng, the Administrative Inspector of Jiji District, along with Section Chief Li of the provincial government to investigate the truth in order to resolve the matter. Yin and Li left Beiping by long-distance bus on the 21st. The people of Yutian, having suffered a great calamity, sent eight representatives, including the president of the Chamber of Commerce, to the province yesterday to petition, demanding that a large army be sent to suppress the rebellion as soon as possible, so as to prevent the rebels from gathering more and more. According to the provincial government's investigation, Shi Yousan is indeed pulling strings behind the scenes of this rebellion. Shi has not moved from Tianjin, but has people coming and going to deliver messages. In addition, Peng Zuyou, the nephew of Peng Shoushen, the former division commander of the Zhili Army, personally arrived at Yayang Hongqiao Town to command everything on behalf of Shi. Peng was bought by the Japanese side during the Tianjin Incident to be the captain of the plainclothes team, willingly working for the tiger. This time, as soon as there was a disturbance, he was eager to try. Yutian is located in a demilitarized zone, and large armies cannot enter. The rebels have gathered more than 2,000 people. The provincial government is concerned that the few security corps and militia in the war zone will not be able to resolve the situation easily. They plan to come up with a good strategy after receiving the reports from Yin Rugeng and Section Chief Li. (January 23rd)

Songjiang

The County Government Welcomes the Handover of Notorious Bandits for Trial

The cases of the notorious bandits Xia Dasan Mazi and others, who gathered together to rob Wu Youlan's family in Punan Zhujiahang, etc., were investigated by Yang Shijie, who was dispatched by the former Public Security Bureau Chief Shen Jing, who purchased information in Shanghai and arrested Xia Dasan Mazi and his wife in the silk factory workshop in Hongkou and escorted them to Songjiang. They confessed that their accomplices, Xia Sanxiao Mazi and others, were still hiding in Pinghu County, Zhejiang Province. Chen Shuliang, the former Chief Inspector, was dispatched to Pinghu with a document to arrest Xia Sanxiao Mazi, his mother Wang, and three other bandits, Wang San San, at their address. One Mauser pistol and one 6-inch pistol were found, along with 161 rounds of ammunition and three bandit ships. Because the magistrate of Pinghu County was in the process of changing hands, no one was responsible, so they were not brought back. Xia Dasan Mazi's wife, who is currently detained in Songjiang, is six months pregnant and gave birth at the county hospital a few days ago. The county government specially dispatched Fei Gongxia, a patrol officer of the water patrol team, to Pinghu with a document to welcome the transfer of the criminals. The three bandits and the seized guns and ammunition have been escorted to Songjiang by Officer Fei today. They have been instructed to be temporarily detained in the county prison. The three bandit ships are expected to arrive in Songjiang tonight.

Tang Guanyu Unveils the Ceremony and Invites Participation from All Sectors

Reduction of U.S. Cotton Loan: Economic Commission Has No Definite News

Cotton Yarn Industry Sources Say:

Or The Deadline May Be Extended

According to Central News Agency, a United Press International telegram from Washington yesterday reported that Jesse Jones, head of the US Federal Loan Administration, said that the US$50 million US cotton and wheat loan signed by Song Ziwen, the former Chinese Minister of Finance, was originally intended to purchase US$40 million worth of cotton and US$10 million worth of wheat. Since the agreement was signed, China has only used US$7 million worth of cotton. By the originally specified expiration date of July 1st, China is unlikely to be able to use US$40 million worth. Therefore, China and the United States are currently seeking ways to reduce the total amount of the US$50 million loan, etc. Yesterday morning, a Central News Agency reporter specially asked Chen Guangfu, chairman of the Cotton Industry Control Committee of the National Economic Commission, about this. Chen was busy with official duties and sent Director Deng to meet the reporter. According to Deng, Chairman Chen had not yet received definite news about the UPI telegram, but had only seen it in the newspapers. The reporter then inquired from sources in the local cotton yarn industry and learned that since former Minister Song went abroad in April of last year to attend the World Economic Conference and signed the US$50 million loan, of which US$40 million was to purchase cotton, with July 1st as the expiration date, only US$7 million has been used so far. This means that by July 1st, there will still be US$33 million worth of cotton that cannot be purchased. The reason is that imports of foreign cotton in our country (including cotton textiles, etc.) amount to 300 million national currency per year, but Japanese and Indian goods account for more than 60% of this. Therefore, it is widely believed that when the July 1st deadline arrives, it will be necessary to extend the deadline, otherwise it will be difficult to purchase the remaining US$33 million worth of cotton. As for the fact that China and the United States are currently seeking ways to reduce the US$50 million loan amount, inquiries from relevant parties in this city, such as the Shanghai office of the National Economic Commission, have all stated that they are unaware of this.

The Outcome of the Huidefeng Labor Strike Mediated by the Party and Government

Five Resolutions Decided

The Assault and Battery Section to Be Prosecuted Separately

The Union Announces Resumption of Work This Morning

According to Da Gong She, Huidefeng Company, a British firm, recently hired Ni Huiyang as a foreman, who led new workers to drive out old workers, triggering a labor strike. The other day, a violent fight occurred due to the forceful seizure of work, escalating into a bloody tragedy. The union immediately petitioned the Party and government authorities for investigation. After the Party and government authorities sent personnel to mediate, it was decided that work would resume this morning. Details are as follows:

Request for the Arrest of the Culprit

All workers of Huidefeng Company, believing that Ni Huiyang, hired by the company, led hooligans to seize work at approximately 6:00 PM the other day, resulting in a tragic fight with many workers injured, were filled with righteous indignation. Yesterday morning, they dispatched representatives, including Zi Ayou, Mao Zhixian, Chen Baofeng, and more than ten others, to petition the Fenglin Bridge Municipal Party Headquarters, requesting the arrest of the troublemaker Ni Huiyang and assistance in resolving the dispute. Huang Tiren of the Civil Affairs Department received them and promised to find a way to mediate. They then went to the Social Affairs Bureau in the city center to petition, where Wang Xianqing received them and promised to work with the Municipal Party Headquarters to handle the matter. Party and Government Mediation

Since all workers were forced to go on strike, Ni Huiyang gathered a large number of hooligans at 5:00 PM the other day, attempting to forcibly seize work, which led to a conflict with the workers and a bloody tragedy. The union immediately petitioned the Party and government authorities for investigation. Yesterday, the Municipal Party Headquarters sent Huang Tiren, and the Social Affairs Bureau sent Zhu Jintao, to the company for mediation. As a result, the company acknowledged: (1) Ni Huiyang is suspended from his position; (2) Workers will no longer be dismissed without reason in the future; (3) Workers will resume work collectively tomorrow morning; (4) There should be no unjustified strikes; (5) When adding workers, the company will hire those recommended by the old supervisors or foremen. As for the conflict case, it will be legally resolved separately with Ni Huiyang.

Injured Workers Sent to Hospital

During the conflict at 6:00 PM the other day, both new and old workers were injured. The new workers had already been sent by the police to the Tongren and Renji hospitals. The injured old workers included Chai Zhenyu from Cibei, Lu Bingqian from Jiangyin, Shi Heqing from Chongming, and Fu Fuchang from Yuyao. These four were sent to the Nanyang Hospital for treatment by the union yesterday. Ningbo native Zhang Qinghua went missing on the scene, and his whereabouts are still unknown.

Resumption of Work This Morning

After the Party and government mediation of the labor strike, it was decided that work would resume tomorrow morning. The union issued a special notice to all workers yesterday, stating: Fellow workers, this labor strike and the bloody tragedy that occurred were purely caused by Ni Huiyang's despicable behavior and illegal actions, which we deeply resent. Now, the Party and government authorities have sent personnel to mediate and decided: (1) The company will dismiss Ni Huiyang; (2) The company acknowledges that it will never dismiss workers in the future; (3) Workers must not strike without reason; (4) The added workers will be hired by the company upon the recommendation of the old supervisors or foremen; (5) Work will resume collectively tomorrow morning. Although Ni Huiyang has been dismissed by the company, his destructive actions and daring to incite a crowd to fight are truly lawless. We will petition the Municipal Party Headquarters to inform the Municipal Public Security Bureau to arrest and bring to justice the ringleaders Ni Huiyang and Niu Qilin, and file a criminal lawsuit in court. We hope that all our members will abide by these decisions and return to work as usual tomorrow morning (i.e., this morning).

"January 28th" Memorial Day as Mass Mobilization Day for Rent Reduction

Leaflets and Slogans Posted Throughout the City

The Shanghai Rent Reduction Committee issued four important letters yesterday, which are recorded as follows:

Mass Mobilization on "January 28th": The Committee sent letters to various organizations in the city yesterday, stating: With the impact of the "January 28th" incident, the Shanghai market has declined, unable to recover, and it is difficult to maintain. To regulate finance, maintain the current situation, and relieve the people's livelihood, reducing rent has become a way to lessen the burden on citizens. We have convened meetings with various organizations to form the Shanghai Rent Reduction Committee. The necessary expenses will be covered by donations of five, ten, twenty, or thirty yuan from various organizations. At the first executive meeting on January 23rd, it was resolved that: (A) The "January 28th" Memorial Day will be designated as the mass mobilization day for rent reduction in the city. At that time, slogans will be distributed, and we request that various organizations distribute them to their affiliated shops and households for posting to promote awareness and achieve maximum effectiveness. (B) The rent reduction movement requires collective wisdom and concerted solidarity. We hereby request that the affiliated branches of various organizations promptly convene citizens' meetings to discuss rent reduction plans. We hope that you will investigate and handle this matter. If there is a scheduled meeting, please inform the committee three days in advance so that we can send personnel to participate. In response to the resolutions, we notify your organization to: (1) Allocate the agreed funds immediately to facilitate progress; (2) Distribute and post leaflets and slogans widely to emphasize publicity; (3) Hold a rent reduction meeting as soon as possible to ensure universal participation and demonstrate its popularity. We hope you will handle this promptly for the public good.

Representative Meeting to Be Held Tomorrow: The Committee separately notified representatives of various organizations yesterday, stating: At the first executive meeting on January 23rd, it was resolved that: the principles of rent reduction and important cases for future action should be approved and implemented by the general assembly of representatives of various organizations. We hereby schedule a representative meeting for Friday, January 26th, at 2:00 PM at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's regular meeting room in Tianhou Temple Bridge. We hope that your representative will attend on time to discuss important cases and jointly plan progress. This matter concerns the relief of the people's livelihood, so please do not delay.

Letters of Appointment for Legal Advisors: The Committee sent letters to twenty-seven lawyers, including Xue Du Bi and Ma Junshuo, stating: Our committee is dedicated to upholding the people's livelihood and promoting rent reduction, which is currently actively underway. At the first executive meeting held on January 23rd, it was resolved to establish a legal advisory group and appoint legal experts. We have long admired your profound legal knowledge and sense of justice. It has been decided to appoint you as one of the advisors of the legal advisory group of our committee. We hope that you will agree to take on this role and fulfill your responsibilities in safeguarding legal rights and assisting in the progress of the rent reduction movement, thereby strengthening our public relations.

Letters of Appointment for Secretaries and Staff: The Committee separately sent letters to various secretaries and staff, stating: In accordance with the resolution of the first executive committee meeting on January 20th, you are appointed as a secretary (staff member). We have long admired your enthusiasm for social work. We rely on your efforts to promote the rent reduction movement. Please assume your position immediately to facilitate progress.

Sun Chuanfang Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday

Reportedly a Private Visit

According to Guomin She, Sun Chuanfang, the former commander-in-chief of the Five Provinces Allied Army, has been residing in Tianjin since stepping down and has not engaged in political endeavors for a long time. In the spring of last year, he once sought to escape the world and planned to completely abandon his political life, which caused quite a stir in society. However, various parties, considering Sun to be a veteran general in North China, did not want him to remain idle and invited him to come out of retirement, but Sun would only smile and put his hands together in prayer.
