Educational Status of Anhui Province (4)

｜Inspection Report by Special Commissioner Li Ximou of the Ministry of Education｜

(Ji) "Implementation Status and Opinions of Those in Charge of the Provisional Regulations for the Graduation Examination of Primary and Secondary Schools." When the high school entrance examination was held, disputes arose. However, the results were still implemented according to the original plan. The examination system has both advantages and disadvantages, and everything depends on how the authorities use it. Before the entrance examination in Anhui Province, each subject first drafted several preparatory questions, which was criticized by many people. In fact, this situation is common in most provinces, and the method should not be too strict at the beginning of the entrance examination system. If young students are motivated to study because of the entrance examination, then the examination system has achieved its goal. (The Provincial Education Department has prepared various statistics on the entrance examination situation in primary and secondary schools, which are omitted here.) The opinions of the person in charge of the province regarding the entrance examination are summarized as follows: (1) Handling the entrance examination affairs is extremely complicated, and it is even more difficult to hold them in a centralized manner. The complexity of the procedures, such as the allocation of examination papers, examination questions, and examination venues, is beyond words. The waste of time and money is secondary. In order to make it easy and convenient, the procedures for reporting from various schools should be simplified, but this kind of decentralized method seems to be easier on a small scale. The examination time should also be advanced, preferably in late May, because it is too hot in July, the government office hours are shortened, and students gather in large numbers, which can easily cause diseases. (2) The entire province should use the same teaching materials, and it is appropriate to designate reference books for examination questions, so that students can have a basis for practice. When creating questions, it is appropriate to create more essay questions and fewer test questions. The questions should focus on the big picture and emphasize understanding, while avoiding unnecessary memorization. There should be a large number of questions, more than ten in each subject, so that the teaching materials covered are wider and there is an opportunity to choose answers. (3) In calculating grades, daily grades should not be included to avoid malpractice. (4) The re-examination method is cumbersome and inconvenient to handle. Students also feel that there are many difficulties in waiting for the re-examination, which is very costly, and because the time is tight, the traffic is

inconvenient, which hinders the college entrance examination. The method should be improved urgently. (5) In the organization of the graduation examination committee for primary and secondary school students, in addition to the assistant examination committee members, there should be chief examiners and invigilators. The chief examiners should be responsible for the chief examination affairs in each district, the assistant examination committee members should be responsible for drafting questions and grading papers, and the invigilators should be responsible for invigilation. (6) Primary and secondary school graduates often prepare for the entrance examination day and night, and work too hard, which affects their health. The development of primary school children is not yet complete, and the harm is even greater. (7) All parties in the province believe that after the department holds the high school entrance examination and grades are determined, it takes time, and it is difficult to handle the re-examination, and the candidates also feel that waiting for the re-examination is costly, and because of the urgency of time, the traffic is

inconvenient, which hinders the entrance examination, and methods should be sought to provide relief. According to the department's opinion, this article should be changed to the regulations for high school students' entrance examination in accordance with Articles 64 and 65 of the High School Regulations, and students who fail to pass all subjects in the examination should not graduate. If there are subjects that fail in three or more subjects or only two subjects fail, but the subjects are any two of the four subjects of Chinese, English, mathematics, and nature in junior high school, or any three of the five subjects of Chinese, English, mathematics, physics, and chemistry in high school, the students should repeat the grade for one year. If there is one subject that fails or although there are two subjects that fail, but the subjects are not as stipulated above, the students should be ordered to take a re-examination once. However, these students may be issued a certificate by the department and bureau to take the high school or vocational school examination first. After being admitted, they will be treated as probationary students, and after participating in the next graduation examination, they will be given a graduation certificate after passing the re-examination of the failed subjects, which can only be used as a formal student after verification by the school where they studied. (8) Students' families and society support the examination system, but because of the phenomena and problems described in item 6, there are many requests to improve or abolish the primary school entrance examination method, and at the very least, it cannot be consistent with the high school entrance examination method, and there are many suggestions for holding an examination for university graduates in order to standardize the level of university students.

(9) Free methods, scholarships and improvement suggestions. In addition to scholarships for studying abroad at public expense and scholarships from domestic universities, normal schools and women's vocational schools are exempt from tuition and meal fees, and vocational schools for men and women are exempt from tuition fees. The intention of this scholarship and free method is good, and the initial effect is also great, but after a long time, the situation of the times has changed, and the drawbacks have arisen, and it seems necessary to revise it. The various scholarships and free methods are listed below: (A) "Provincial Primary and Secondary School Free Method", (1) Free method for students with excellent grades. Each student in the province's high school pays 20 yuan per year for tuition, 10 yuan per year for junior high school, and 3 yuan per year for senior primary school. It is now stipulated that there are three free places in each class, and those who are ranked in the top three in the total average of each semester are exempt from tuition fees. (2) Method of exempting tuition fees for students in disaster areas in the 22nd academic year. The province has a method of exempting tuition fees for disaster areas such as Liu'an, Huoshan, Huoqiu, and Fuyang this year. All students in the province's provincial high school whose families in their original place of origin have been directly harmed by bandits and are unable to pay fees can be exempted from tuition fees with proof from the county government of their original place of origin. However, this method is temporarily limited to this year. (B) "Methods and quotas for scholarships abroad." It has been found that the province has always had a subsidy item for students studying abroad at their own expense, which is listed in the province's local budget. In the autumn of the 17th year of the Republic of China, due to the determination of the regulations for studying abroad, this subsidy item was changed to a scholarship, and eleven regulations for scholarships for Anhui students studying abroad at their own expense were formulated and reported to the provincial government and the Ministry of Education for record. This scholarship stipulates that there are seven countries with vacancies: (1) The United Kingdom has a fixed quota of eight, with each student receiving 8 pounds of English money per month. (2) Germany and Austria have a total of 13, with each student receiving 120 marks of German currency per month. (3) France and Belgium have a total of 22, with each student receiving 500 francs of French currency per month. (4) The United States has 12, with each student receiving 40 US dollars per month. (5) Japan has 15, with each student receiving 40 yen per month. The total amount is 70, and the annual cost is approximately 97,000 yuan. () The scholarship for each student is approximately half of the provincial expenses.) The procedures for checking and supplementing should be based on the regulations that students who have been admitted to a famous university for one year and have excellent grades must also submit a certificate of academic performance issued by the president of the school and a self-filled registration form to the department for review and registration. After confirming the vacancy, it will be submitted for summary review and supplement, and the scholarship will be issued from the month it is approved. It has been found that the Ministry of Education has ordered all provinces to revise the existing regulations for scholarships for students studying abroad at public expense and at their own expense. Since public-funded students need to take preliminary and follow-up tests to show seriousness, it seems that students studying abroad at their own expense should also be tested in China. The province now plans to set the amount of each scholarship according to the talents needed by the province, and set the questions according to the examination method for public-funded students (emphasizing science, agriculture, engineering, and medicine). After the department passes the examination, it will report to the Ministry of Education for record, and ask for the issuance of a study abroad certificate, allowing them to study abroad, and then change the name to half-public-funded students, and the monthly tuition fee will be issued at half the rate of public-funded students. (Regulations will be formulated separately.) (C) "Loans from various counties". The province had previously issued repeated orders to stop the practice of students' subsidies and sightseeing fees from various counties, as it hindered the progress of local primary schools. Later, the counties reported that many of the students from the counties studying at various universities were poor, and asked for separate regulations to be issued to provide university students with loans. The department considered the matter to be feasible and approved the request, and ordered the formulation of loan methods to show restrictions, but this kind of regulation is based on local financial resources. If funds are not sufficient, it is still not allowed to be established. In fact, it is different from scholarships and subsidies in name, and the designated funds are limited, so it does not seem to have much to do with it. Counties that have established loans include Liu'an, Wangjiang, Shitai, Fuyang, Suxian, Qianshan, Taihu, Mengcheng, Fanchang, and Dangtu. (D) "Scholarships for domestic universities." Eleven regulations have been formulated regarding the method of awarding scholarships to domestic universities, which can focus on academic performance and subjects. Unfortunately, special consideration for poor children has not been specifically mentioned, which seems to be a shortcoming. The Anhui Education Department has scholarships for students studying at domestic universities, including 35 quotas at Central University, 2 at Shanghai Medical College, Shanghai Business College, (3), Zhongshan University, (2), Peking University, (8), Beiping Normal University, (10), Peking University Engineering College, (5), Peking University Agricultural College, (2), Peking University Medical College, (3), Peking University Law School, (3), Peking University Women's

College of Arts and Sciences, (5), Peking University Business College, (2), Peking University Art College, (2), Tsinghua University, (10), Beiyang Institute of Technology, (6), Wuhan University, (12), Zhejiang University, (3), Tongji University, (5), Jinan

University, (3), Hangzhou Art College, (1), Music College, (1), Jiaotong University, (10), Jiaotong University School of Civil Engineering, (5), Jiaotong University Beiping Railway Management College, (3), Nankai University, (5), Fudan University, (5), Guanghua University, (4), Daxia University, (4), Yanjing University, (5), Union Medical College, (2), Jinling University, (12), Nantong College Textile Department, (2). Each of the above receives 110 yuan per year. (E) "Suggestions for improving free and scholarship policies." The Education Department has the following suggestions for improving the scholarship and free methods: (1) The number of free places should be the same throughout the province. Each county's senior primary school should stipulate the number of free places for students with excellent grades. Provincial high schools (normal and vocational schools have no tuition fees) should be stipulated by the province. The number of free places should be determined by examination results. This free place is mainly to exempt tuition fees, and other expenses should be paid as usual. (2) Poverty scholarships should be established. Counties should set up poverty scholarships, limited to senior primary schools and junior vocational schools. The province should set up poverty scholarships, limited to secondary schools and vocational schools. Provincial universities should also set up poverty scholarships. This scholarship is divided into half-fee and full-fee (including tuition, meals and accommodation fees. (3) Students with poverty scholarships should be strictly examined to obtain them, and they should be strictly managed when they enter the school. (4) Students with scholarships to study abroad should also obtain them through examinations. (5) Domestic scholarship students should be effectively managed by the original school to determine performance standards.

(10) Inspection Notes. School inspections, regarding books, instruments, classrooms, cleanliness, etc., which are superficial are obvious. Regarding teaching methods, moral education guidance, and the school spirit, it is not easy to be accurate about the impression unless a long period of inspection is obtained. This inspection in Anhui only lasted for more than 20 days, and it is inevitable that it cannot be detailed. Schoolwork, the situation of the school, the advantages and disadvantages of the teaching methods of teachers, etc., are all based on the impressions obtained by chance in a very short period of inspection. It can be imagined that it is rash. The following kinds of things are all offered in good faith, and please do not criticize them with malice. As the saying goes, only good people can accept all words, which is what is hoped for the educational authorities of Anhui Province. (The original report lists the situation of the schools inspected, which is omitted due to space limitations.) (End)

Chinese Cultural Advancement Association Holds Inaugural Meeting of Promoters Yesterday

Pan Gongzhan and others were elected as preparatory committee members.

The preparation time is limited to two weeks.

The Chinese Cultural Advancement Association, initiated by Chen Guofu and others, held an inaugural meeting of promoters at 2:00 PM yesterday at No. 66 Hankou Road. A preparatory committee was immediately elected to organize the preparatory committee and be responsible for the progress of the matter. The details are as follows:

Promoters present: There were more than 100 people, including Pan Gongzhan, Wu Xingya, Tong Xingbai, Ding Mocun, Tao Baichuan, Guo Wei, Ye Xiufeng, Zheng Zhengqiu, Shao Zuiweng, Jiang Jianbai, Chen Bai, Zhou Feicheng, Huang Zaoxiong, Yuan Xueyi, Xu Xingchu, Chen Jicheng, Xu Zexiang, Xue Guangqian, Tang Zengshou, Xu Shaodi, Chen Baohua, Zhang Zhengfan, Long Tiyao, Fang Huanru, Wang Xinming, Huang Xianggu, Kang Xuanyi, Huang Hao, Li Shiqun, Zhou Yuying, Yuan Yeyu, and Tang Huiping. Chen Guofu, Chen Lifu, Ye Chucang, Wu Tiecheng, etc. were unable to attend due to attending the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee.

Chairman's report: The meeting began at 2:00 PM. Guo Wei was elected as the temporary chairman and Xu Xingchu as the recorder. After performing the etiquette, the chairman first reported on the situation of the initiation, followed by Pan Gongzhan's report on the significance of organizing the Chinese Cultural Association. He briefly stated that the standard of a country and nation in historical events is based on culture. The foundation of political economy and all undertakings is culture. The construction of all undertakings depends on the spirit, and the power to encourage this spirit is the greatest with culture. Culture not only expresses thoughts, but also transforms thoughts. Therefore, the transformation of human life is all based on culture as the original driving force. Since the Northern Expedition of the National Revolutionary Army, there has been a great revolutionary movement, and the power of its occurrence is due to the fact that Mr. Sun Yat-sen, since the founding of the Tongmenghui, has been engaged in ideological transformation and guidance, giving the nation a new life and strength. In other words, culture is the basic strength to promote it. However, because in the process of revolution, most people pay attention to politics and military affairs, and ignore culture, those in society who are committed to cultural undertakings have embarked on the road of politics and military affairs, so the reactionary factions seize the cultural tools by chance, so the revolutionary forces are developing day by day, and the reactionary propaganda of the Communist Party is also spreading day by day, especially in recent years. Therefore, we initiate this meeting to promote and revive the national culture on the one hand to build our theory, and to eliminate the reactionary theory that does not meet the needs of our country on the other hand.

Election of the Preparatory Committee: Then discuss the matters. (1) It was decided that the number of preparatory committee members should be 11, and Pan Gongzhan, Ding Mocun, Guo Wei, Jiang Jianbai, Zheng Zhengqiu, Tong Xingbai, Zhu Yingpeng, Li Zhiyun, Zhu Yinong, Fang Huanru, Chen Bai and other 11 people were elected as preparatory committee members, and Ding Mocun and Guo Wei were the conveners of the preparatory committee. (2) The task of the preparatory committee is to be responsible for all the progress from the closing of the initiators' meeting to the establishment of the general assembly. (3) The declaration of the association will be temporarily based on the origin of the creation, and the initiators can submit written opinions to Mr. Ding Mocun to the preparatory committee within five days. (4) The preparation period should not exceed two weeks at most. (5) All those present today and the initiators published in the previous newspapers are

the initiators of the association. After the meeting, the meeting was adjourned and the photos were taken.

Successful Resolution of the Jinda Disturbance

Acting President Shen Pengfei to Arrive in Shanghai to Assume Duties Soon

Students' Attitude Has Softened, Expressing Welcome to Shen

(Shanghai News Agency) The disturbance at National Jinan University, since its occurrence, has lasted for a month now. The Ministry of Education has already decided on a solution, sending Zheng Hongnian to Nanyang to inspect overseas Chinese education, while school affairs will be managed by Shen Pengfei, Director of the Higher Education Department of the Ministry of Education, as acting president. The students' attitude has become more moderate and they welcome Shen. Details are as follows:

Order from the Ministry of Education: Zheng Hongnian received Instruction No. 789 from the Ministry of Education on January 23rd, stating, "You are hereby assigned to Nanyang to inspect overseas Chinese education and raise funds for National Jinan University. This order is to be followed." It is reported that Shen will arrive in Shanghai soon to take over duties, and since he cannot handle the duties of Director of the Higher Education Department concurrently, Minister Wang will appoint someone to act in his place temporarily.

Letter from the Board of Directors: The Jinda Board of Directors sent a letter to Zheng Hongnian yesterday, stating, "Respectfully informing you that the Board of Directors of this school held a meeting on the 19th of this month to discuss and resolve the disturbance, deciding to send President Zheng to Nanyang to inspect overseas Chinese education and raise funds for Jinda. During your absence, please have the Ministry of Education send someone to maintain school affairs. Regarding the students who initiated this disturbance, please have the Ministry of Education investigate and deal with them strictly." It is hoped that this letter, along with the recorded details, will be reviewed. Respectfully, Sun Ke, Standing Director.

Student Expression: The school's student organization to protect the school and expel Zheng will convene a meeting today

in the morning and plans to hold a

general student assembly tomorrow to discuss everything. It is reported that the students are satisfied with the Ministry of Education's decision and their attitude has softened. They also welcome Director Shen's acting presidency, so the school disturbance can be considered over.

Zheng's Remarks: According to Zheng Hongnian's remarks to reporters yesterday,

"Since the disturbance occurred at Jinda, I have stated to the Board of Directors that I will (1) not interfere, (2) not resign, (3) not take leave, (4) not recommend someone to act in my place, and (5) not want the school to be dissolved. Now, the Ministry of Education has assigned Director Shen to act as president. Shen has many years of experience in education and should be able to handle it with ease. I have already sent a telegram to welcome him. The faculty and staff whom the students wanted to expel have also resigned from their positions. This matter can be considered over. I hope the students will focus on their studies and make up the exams. All handover procedures within the school were completed ten days ago. From now on, I will not manage school affairs in any way and hope that no one, whether from inside or outside the school, will come to discuss school matters with me again. As for the Ministry of Education sending me to Nanyang to inspect overseas Chinese education, I was not informed beforehand and have no intention of going at present."

Ministry of Education Orders Shanghai's Four Night Schools to Stop Enrolling New Students

Orders Schools to Close in Phases

There is no Immediate Closure

Regarding a news item about the Ministry of Education ordering Shanghai Jiang, Chi Zhi, the School of Law and Political Science, and the Business School to stop running night schools, it has been learned that the Ministry of Education, considering the establishment of night schools, has many inconveniences in terms of military training and student self-study, so it has ordered the schools not to enroll new night school students or transfer students from the next semester. As for current students, the schools will close in phases, and there will be no problems with the qualifications of current students. As for whether the schools receiving the order are limited to the aforementioned four schools, this has not yet been confirmed.

Educator Yang Pingyu Passes Away

Mr. Yang Pingyu, former section chief and supervisor of the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, and former professor of the Second Jiangsu Provincial Normal School and principal of the attached elementary school, served in the education field for more than thirty years. His scholarship and morality were admired by society. Due to old age and declining health, he passed away from illness at 6:00 AM on the 23rd of this month. The Shanghai education community and the Longmen Alumni Association and other groups plan to launch a memorial service to express their condolences.

County Elementary School Mandarin Exhibition Opens Today

The Shanghai County Education Bureau, taking advantage of the winter vacation, has scheduled a three-day Mandarin exhibition for all elementary schools in the county from today (the 25th) to the 27th, held at the Beiqiao Elementary School in the new county seat. After drafting plans, designated schools in each district were asked to prepare and collect exhibits from various schools and send them to the venue. Yesterday, the bureau sent staff to arrange the exhibits from the schools in each district in the east and west classrooms and the assembly hall of Beiqiao Elementary School. There are dozens of exhibits from each school, such as diaries, notebooks, novels, stories, poems, letters, dictation, phonetic symbols in large and small characters, as well as reading methods, teaching methods, composition teaching, calligraphy, etc. for elementary and advanced Mandarin courses. They are all excellent works from various schools. The bureau has also hired judges to review them starting today, so as to select the best for awards to encourage them. At the same time, schools will notify their students to visit the venue.

Zhu Mingxin Discusses the Situation of Gansu College

Zhu Mingxin, Dean of Gansu College, came to Shanghai on official business the other day. According to him, this trip to Shanghai represents President Wang Jinghuai in raising books from major bookstores. He has already contacted various bookstores and achieved good results. The managers of the bookstores, recognizing the backwardness of culture in the Northwest, have all agreed to donate. When asked about the Ministry of Education's reorganization of the college, he said that this concerned the internal organization of the college. Because the college's organization still used the old system, which was largely inconsistent with the ministry's orders, the outline was re-established and submitted to the ministry for approval. However, the outline took too much into account the local situation, which led to its rejection by the Ministry of Education. In fact, the college had already implemented all the points indicated by the Ministry of Education.

Nankai Alumni in Shanghai Host Banquet for President Zhang Boling

Zhang Boling, President of Tianjin Nankai School, arrived in Shanghai on the 22nd evening due to school affairs, the details of which were reported in yesterday's newspaper. The Nankai Alumni Association of this city held a banquet at the YMCA in Ba Xian Qiao at 5 PM the day before yesterday to welcome him. More than a hundred alumni of the school attended. During the banquet, Zhang gave a speech, saying that he had been greatly stimulated by observing current affairs in recent years. After introspection, he believes that the greatest concern of our country is that everyone cannot abandon their personal opinions and unite and cooperate. The nation has reached a critical juncture of life and death. If we do not wake up, we will be eliminated by the world forever. His words were filled with emotion. Then, Zheng Tonghe reported on the recent work of the alumni association. It was decided on the spot to raise scholarship funds for the alma mater, plan a meeting place, and compile an alumni directory. After the banquet, a movie was filmed to commemorate the occasion. The gathering ended happily at 8 PM that night.

Shanghai Alumni Association of Shude Middle School Established

Shude Middle School in Suzhou has been established for more than ten years and has achieved remarkable results. Many graduates have come to Shanghai to work. In the past, Shanghai alumni Zhu Mingyu and others, in order to connect alumni's feelings and study academics, initiated the organization of the Shanghai Alumni Association of Suzhou Shude Middle School. Preparations have been underway for a year. A founding meeting was held at 3 PM the day before yesterday in the conference hall of the Silk Industry Bank Building on San Ma Road in this city. More than thirty members, including Li Li, Cheng Jingrong, and Gu Xuefan, attended. Li Lingyu presided over the meeting. First, the articles of association were approved, and then the first session of officers was elected. Cheng Jiazhen, Zhu Mingyu, Xu Chang, Li Lingyu, and Cheng Zongxian were elected as executive committee members, and Gu Qingshi, Li Zhuoyu, and Yang Shanchang were elected as supervisory committee members.

Weiyu Elementary School Expands its Campus

Weiyu Elementary School in this city was founded by well-known industrialists Mu Ouchu, Liu Hongsheng, Huang Yanfang, Zou Bingwen, Pan Lunxu, and Wang Zhixin. Yang Weiyu serves concurrently as the principal. Teaching and management are strict, the curriculum is practical, and ability-based classes are implemented, with emphasis on individual teaching. It has been well-received by society. Now, because the original rented school buildings are insufficient, it has moved to a new campus at No. 561 La Fei De Road, west end of Lu Ban Road. The architecture is exquisite and the campus is spacious. Its complete facilities are rare among private elementary schools. Enrollment is scheduled for February 2nd and school starts on the 3rd. Boarding students are also being accepted.

Recent News from Huacheng Tutorial School

The curriculum of the Huacheng Tutorial School in Yinhe Lane, French Concession, Fangbang Bridge, is the same as that of ordinary primary and secondary schools, but the subjects are limited to essential ones to meet social needs. Sports

Ministry of Education's Physical Education Committee

More Than Ten Proposals to be Discussed at Today's Meeting

(Nanjing, 24th) The Physical Education Committee of the Ministry of Education is scheduled to meet on the 25th afternoon to discuss more than ten proposals. The key proposals include: (1) All levels of schools nationwide should have uniform regulations for athletic competitors; (2) Establish regulations for the certification of elementary school physical education teachers and implement them as soon as possible; (3) Establish regulations for the salary advancement of primary and secondary school physical education teachers; (4) Establish a National Sports University; (5) Unify the national school sports organization system; (6) Organize a national summer physical education refresher course; (7) Prepare to attend the next World Games as soon as possible. This will be the first regular meeting after the second reorganization of the Physical Education Committee of the Ministry of Education, scheduled to be held at the Ministry of Education this afternoon (the 25th).

Seven members of the standing committee, such as Chu Minyi, Zhang Zhijiang, Wu Yunrui, Cheng Dengke, Hao Gengsheng, etc., are all in Nanjing and will attend as scheduled. Others, such as Yuan Dunli in Beiping and Shen Siliang in Shanghai, will also attend at the time. The issues to be discussed at this meeting include how to prepare for the Far Eastern Games, as well as budget estimates and preliminary locations, all of which will be discussed by the committee. The holding of physical education refresher courses this summer will also be discussed in advance, and the establishment of a sports school will be further studied to promote its early realization. It is reported that all proposals of the Ministry of Education are being sorted out to be submitted to the meeting for discussion.

World Sprint Phenomenon Tolan Gives Up Athletic Life

Feeling the Pain of Unemployment

Determined to Work Hard

World sprint phenomenon, African-American Eddie Tolan, will announce his retirement and no longer appear on the track, determined to work hard at his profession. Tolan is the Olympic champion in the 100m and 200m. He studied medicine at the University of Michigan. His retirement from the athletic field is not due to any particular dissatisfaction, but simply to find a job. Last autumn, he sought jobs everywhere but failed. Therefore, he had to return to his hometown of Tiddeloa. The second day the Olympian arrived home, he encountered a welcoming band and his cousin Footland. Foot is a laborer. Tolan was so touched by the scene that he thought that although his cousin's position was humble, he had a job, while he could not even support his parents. Completing his medical studies would only be interrupted, and becoming a famous doctor would only be a dream.

After graduating from the University of Michigan for four years, he became a world sprint star. The day before participating in the Olympic preliminaries, he wrote to his mother, saying that if he became a champion, the family's situation could gradually improve from then on.

Now Tolan has found a place. As a secretary in an agency, he has somewhat fulfilled his wishes. Eddie told people, "I am confident that I will no longer race. From now on, I will work hard at my profession. The walls of gold and silver medals, is that all it is worth?"

Four Players From the Liangjiang Team Were Sent Off

The results of last night's West Youth women's basketball games showed that the Liangjiang beauties continued to win. Liangjiang defeated Southeast A 25-15. The American women defeated the Red team 25-22. In the game between Liangjiang and Southeast, the fouls on both sides were countless. As many as four players from the Liangjiang team were sent off. (1) Liangjiang Wins Southeast A 25-15

(3) McLing Wins Yellow Team 17-12

Yang Sen, Chen Rongming, Chen Baixue, and Shi Ruixia were all sent off one after another. Fortunately, on the Southeast side, main players Liao Zhuyuan and Li Yinan were also sent off, and their fighting power was also weak. Otherwise, Liangjiang would have suffered an accident. The large number of players sent off set an unprecedented record in women's basketball games. Initially, Pan Meng scored first, opening the record. Liao Zhuyuan scored one point on a free throw. Liangjiang took the lead 2-1. Liangjiang continued to score five points. Southeast remained the same. After 10-4 in the first quarter, Southeast relied on Liao Erfeng to enter and exit the basket and chased to 12-10, only two points behind. Unfortunately, it stopped again, and at 17-10, Yang Sen was sent off. At 19-10, Shi Ruixia was also sent off. The first half ended at 21-11, with Liangjiang taking the lead. Starting in the second half, Southeast could not take advantage of Liangjiang's wavering opportunity to attack, and its own fouls were also numerous. At 22-11, Southeast's Li Yinan and Liao Zhuyuan were also sent off. At 25-11, Chen Rongming was sent off. In the last eight minutes, Southeast was still sluggish, even though the opponent was all reserves. The result was a 25-15 victory.

Special Items

Report on Vocational Education from the Ministry of Education Commissioner's Trip to Europe (11)

(5) School Visit Records

French vocational education observation locations: Paris, Nancy, and three locations in Lyon. Lyon is France's largest industrial area, so vocational education is quite developed. In terms of population, Lyon ranks second in the country.

Paris

(1) (Paris Municipal) This school is a vocational school under the Paris municipality.

Established in 1886, it mainly teaches furniture manufacturing, divided into two departments: 1. Furniture Department: (1) Cabinet making, (2) Table making, (3) Wood carving, (4) Curtain weaving. 2. Metalworking Department: (1) Sculpture, applied to bronzes, gems, jewelry, etc., (2) Model making. The workshop area within the school

is 4,800 square meters. Facilities include drawing and sketching studios, woodworking and metalworking shops, and various manufacturing equipment workshops. The equipment is very new and complete. Education focuses on students' aesthetic training, so that the structure of patterns can be unique and different from the mundane, while being pleasing to the eye. For each item of equipment

manufacturing process, it must begin with a pattern, from the pattern to material selection, from the material to color matching, and then to completion. Therefore, it is innovative and practical. Admission requires an examination, including subjects such as French, calculation, and drawing. Admitted students are all primary school graduates, and some have studied in higher primary schools. The age is about 13 to 14 years old. The course is divided into three years, with examinations every year. Those who fail are asked to withdraw from school. Excellent graduates who wish to stay at school for further study have a special class in the following year. Currently, 40% of graduates stay at school to attend the fourth year of classes. Each week's coursework is 54 hours. The morning is for general education and engineering theory classes, and the afternoon is for workshop practice, accounting for 30 hours. Workshop practice instructors are allowed to hold concurrent positions outside the school that are related to their duties. School workshop practice strives to match factory conditions, so when students use machinery in practice, the time required for each action must be recorded by the students. This is a common key point in the training of French apprentice schools. The school is responsible for introducing students to employment, so the principal has close ties with the factory sector, and it is easier to help students find employment.

Three-year graduates are given a Certificat d'Apprentissgelh rh . Graduates are awarded a Diplome. Students residing in Paris are free of charge, while those residing in the suburbs pay 300 francs per year, and students from other provinces pay 700 francs per year.

(2) School of Book Trades. This school is run by the Paris Municipality and is a world-renowned school for printing and bookbinding. Established in 1889, it was initially very simple, but gradually developed. It now offers 15 vocational courses related to the book trade, with the aim of training skilled workers specializing in book trade crafts. Admission requirements are primary school graduation, but students must pass an entrance examination, aged 13 (4) to 17 (8) years old. After graduation, a apprentice certificate is given. The instructors in the school are selected through open competition, regardless of nationality, and are all experts in art and crafts. The entrance examination subjects are (1) dictation, (2) arithmetic, (3) sketching, and a medical examination to determine whether they are suitable for vocational work. At the beginning of admission, students are required to tour various workshops to choose the one they like, and given a few days of trial learning to determine their suitability based on their skills and work. Poor students are exempt from lunch fees, subsidized by the city council. For poor children with excellent grades, living expenses are also provided. Students residing in Paris are also free of charge, while those residing in the suburbs are given 300 francs per student per year with the approval of the local council, and students from other provinces pay 600 francs per year. The school's curriculum emphasizes both theory and practice, especially focusing on patterns. Lithography, wood carving, leather decoration, cork carving, copper engraving, etc., all use patterns as a basic subject. However, those who study other professions also pay attention to geometry and color science. Practical subjects account for 30 hours per week in the first year, 33 hours in the second year, and 36 hours per week in the third and fourth years. Those who fail the year-end exam are asked to withdraw from school. Employers and workers in the printing industry are represented on the examination committee. General subjects include history, geography, national language, science (physics and chemistry), mathematics (arithmetic, algebra, geometry), accounting, outline of laws, outline of rational factory organization, history of art, sketching (plaster, objects, human body), plant and animal research, decorative construction, etc. The courses are as follows: 1. Lithography, divided into four subjects: color printing, lithographic patterns, stone carving, and lithographic plate making. 2. Sculpture, divided into four subjects: wood carving, copperplate engraving, soft paste engraving, and plate making. 3. Photography, divided into three subjects: photography, photographic plate making, and color portraits. 4. Bookbinding, divided into two subjects: installation and leather decoration.

Shen Bao Domestic Goods Weekly

Words of Contribution

To Enthusiastic People from All Over the Country Who Support Domestic Goods

— Yang Yi

Promoting domestic goods is not limited to one corner, but requires efforts from all over the country to be effective. This year has been officially designated as the Women's Domestic Goods Year, and many people say: "This year, it seems only the people in Shanghai are putting in effort, while people in other places are still silent. Is this year Shanghai's Women's Domestic Goods Year?" The reporter was stunned upon hearing this, but later thought that the women's domestic goods movement indeed had the shortcoming of not being widespread. I think men and women from all over the country must also be thinking: it is clearly the national Women's Domestic Goods Year, why is it only lively in Shanghai? Will the other places simply not respond and give up? If there are passionate people with vigor and perseverance, they will definitely not stand idly by, and even more certainly will not be indifferent. I believe that local propaganda movements in various places are certainly important, but the most practical method is to establish domestic goods companies, serving as the central hub for promoting domestic goods in practice. Currently, the China National Products Company has a national joint office established at No. 1 Yuanmingyuan Road, and is in the process of separately contacting people from all over the country to establish China National Products Companies. All methods are very comprehensive, and there are detailed standards for all metropolitan areas and major trading ports. Therefore, I would like to introduce it below, hoping that enthusiastic people from all over the country will unite and open such domestic goods companies that benefit both themselves and others. In our ideal, at least 20 domestic goods companies should appear across the country this year.

Domestic Goods Talk

Women's Year for Being Scolded

— Ms. Ai Ci

Opening up various newspapers regarding "Women's Domestic Goods Year", it seems that the authors are standing on a battle line, launching a general attack on the women's community: saying that last year's "Domestic Goods Year" had no results, and it was all the result of women not using domestic goods, and there is a statistic that 1.4 million foreign imported lipsticks and perfumes in ten months, to prove women's extravagance. If this kind of style does not change, I think it is better to rename it as "Women's Year for Being Scolded" rather than "Women's Domestic Goods Year", which would be more straightforward.

Men and women are all citizens. The name "Women's Domestic Goods Year" is fundamentally humorous. When it comes to domestic goods, no one can deny that we use domestic goods for all our clothing, food, housing, and transportation. There is almost no one, how heartbreaking to say! Does the infant formula eaten by children one day after birth have domestic goods? Is everyone's clothing entirely domestic goods? Are the houses we live in and the appliances we use all domestic goods? The more convenient the transportation, the more railways, highways, and airways are opened, are the trains, cars, and airplanes completely domestic goods? Do you know how much money was sent to foreign countries in the "National Salvation Through Aviation" movement? I think do not use the number of 1.4 million to create the data for the "Women's Year for Being Scolded", because this is not the fundamental way to promote domestic goods.

I remember someone said, "Europeans and Americans create, Japanese imitate, Chinese do not create", but now we can be slightly optimistic: there are indeed many imitations. Go into the domestic goods company and see, aren't there good achievements on display? Originally, as long as it is Chinese capital and Chinese manufacturing, even if the raw materials are completely foreign goods, it meets the prescribed standards for domestic goods. Shouldn't it be considered patriotic to buy and use them? The manuscript paper I am using now is also a domestic product, produced by Tianzhang, but someone said: "You are not completely patriotic if you think like this. Do you really know that no foreign raw materials are used? The more you promote domestic goods with foreign raw materials, the more money flows to foreign countries, isn't it? This is just a difference between fifty steps and a hundred steps." Of course, there is probably no country in the world that is self-sufficient in raw materials, but now the country that relies on foreign supply of raw materials the most is probably us. We can imitate, which is a step forward. I hope the production sector will take another step forward, seek self-sufficiency in raw materials, create completely domestic goods, and the selling price can be cheap, and more people will definitely buy it; otherwise, it will be useless to set a "×× Domestic Goods Year" every year!

Love and Respect Local Goods and Thoroughly Promote Domestic Goods

— Yin Ge

Since the sounds of cannons at Beida Camp, the Chinese people have competed to think of ways to resist. The airplanes in Shenyang were seized, so they resisted with over-mountain guns and grenades, with rifles and machine guns, and finally advocated resistance with broadswords, and even with stones. China's armed resistance gradually promoted local goods. In my opinion, this armed resistance must use the latest and most modern methods. Airplanes, poison gas, artillery, submarines, tanks, etc., these are modern methods of resistance. If these methods cannot be adopted, it is better to honestly not resist.

As for economic resistance, it is very different. Economic resistance is promoting domestic goods. The more local, the better, the more local, the more wonderful. The benefit and wonderfulness of Gandhi in India lies in weaving local cloth, three big characters. Japanese industrial manufacturing is already feared by Western countries, but the country still desperately uses local goods. Our Chinese manufacturing industry is not yet developed. If all the things needed for clothing, food, housing, and transportation do not use the original local goods of this country, it will absolutely not be able to be self-sufficient. For example, in clothing, if you don't wear silk or local cloth, then you must wear foreign goods or Sino-foreign hybrids. For example, in food, if you don't eat granulated sugar, you must eat Japanese white sugar. (Very few Western goods recently) For example, in housing, if you don't want to live in Chinese-style houses constructed of cedar wood, you will definitely live in Western-style houses constructed of foreign pine. I am not opposing Westernization, but I am saying that while China's industry is not yet developed, please Westernize slowly. If everyone can recognize the principle that the more local, the better, you must first have a heart of loving and respecting local goods. In this way, even if you cannot localize everything into domestic goods, you can at least resist some foreign aggression. Fortunately, this kind of victory is as sure as can be. Without a doubt, one point of local goods has one point of benefit. In short, the more local, the more victorious. Therefore, I say that armed resistance, the more local, the more it fails. Economic resistance, the more local, the more it succeeds.

The people of Guangdong are most stimulated by foreign countries. They were also the earliest to promote domestic goods. The slogan they used at first was also to promote local goods. Please take a look at the Sincere and Wing On department stores on Nanjing Road, isn't it clearly written that they sell both foreign and local goods?

Women's Talk on Domestic Goods

Telling Sisters the Enthusiasm for Promoting Domestic Goods Fifteen Years Ago

— Pan Yin Ge

When the author was the principal of a commercial school in his hometown in the seventh or eighth year of the Republic of China, I was very enthusiastic about promoting domestic goods at this time. I advised students to purchase and use domestic goods, and at the same time organized domestic goods stores to sell domestic goods. I set an example myself, not only wearing clothes made entirely of domestic goods, but also using domestic goods for everything in my home. There was a ridiculous thing at the time. That is, I even lit an old-fashioned vegetable oil lamp to read at night. Not only did I not use electric lights, but I did not use Mobil oil lamps. I had a very persevering thought in this. At that time, I was affected by the European War on the one hand; and stimulated by Japan's "self-sufficiency" doctrine on the other hand. At that time, I saw a story about the copper king Torawiemon in a Japanese magazine. Although this Torawi-san was a wealthy man in Japan, his personal life was very frugal. He used an old-fashioned wind lamp to read at night. This biography also praised him for having "unyielding integrity". And there was a photo, which was a picture of Torawi-san sitting on the ground, reading by the wind lamp. The author admired it very much after reading it. So I changed to using the most authentic domestic product - vegetable oil lamps - to read at night. At that time, I also read the story of Gandhi in India while reading. Gandhi resented that India's transportation equipment was taken over by the British, so when he went out, he didn't talk about efficiency, but still rode in an old-fashioned Indian wooden boat. At that time, the author wrote an essay in a magazine in his hometown, promoting domestic goods. There were two sentences in the middle that quoted the above two stories. He said: "When learning from Torawi's wind lamp, reserve strength before it is too late. Do not be like Gandhi's wooden boat, leaving regrets after it is too late." Although the sentences were not well written, it is conceivable that the individual believed in and the determination of the idea at that time.

Such a rustic person later came to Shanghai to work, and was stimulated and besieged a lot, and some things gradually invaded my body, such as felt hats and Serge. Shanghai people's worship of foreign goods and contempt for local customs and goods are indeed the best in the country. This is the illusion created in the past ninety years or so since the opening of trade. Last year, the promotion of domestic goods was named Domestic Goods Year. Although men were not specified, men probably have a greater responsibility. The result of the promotion is very ashamed. According to the statistics from January to October, the import surplus has exceeded 600 million yuan. This year is the Women's Domestic Goods Year, and the focus of this responsibility has turned to the general sisters. Let's see how the statistics will be next year. It's dangerous!

Older ladies can keep some old habits. Young girls will do as their mothers and sisters do. Therefore, the focus of Women's Domestic Goods Year is more on middle-aged sisters. How to break the illusion of the past ninety years and do our best to promote the purchase and use of domestic goods is indeed the greatest responsibility of our sisters this year.

Sales of foreign goods are becoming clearer and lighter

Change the strategy and sell domestic products

All large and small households use domestic goods

Become a rich man in less than three years

Women Should Do Some Serious Work

— Jing Cun

I firmly believe that the women in the Women's Domestic Goods Year should not only be consumers of domestic goods, but also producers of domestic goods. However, the current ladies and young ladies think that it is a humiliating thing to directly participate in the production of domestic goods. It is impossible no matter what. Even if it is possible, they are not willing to do it no matter what. I firmly believe that the women in the Women's Domestic Goods Year, if they cannot directly or indirectly participate in or assist the domestic goods production business, do not deserve to be called a woman in the Women's Domestic Goods Year, and they are sorry to the society for this year's respect for women. At the beginning of the Domestic Goods Year, I once asked the women of this year to show their spirit and make some achievements to show women's ability and comfort the society's desire. Afterwards, I proposed a slogan for women to participate in the domestic goods production business as this year's work goal for women. Now, January of the Women's Domestic Goods Year is gradually passing, where are the achievements that women have shown? Is the Women's Friendship Conference the achievement of the Women's Domestic Goods Year? Is it the achievement of the Women's Domestic Goods Year to ask a lady to ride a horse and direct the procession of the Domestic Goods Movement Parade? Is it the achievement of the Women's Domestic Goods Year to invite one or two socialites to open the Domestic Goods Bazaar or Exhibition? This is not it, that is not it, so what is the real achievement of the Women's Domestic Goods Year? Please write down a few points that I thought of for a while:

(1) All married men dare not buy any more foreign goods to avoid their wives' scolding.

(2) Children all know that using domestic goods is the responsibility of citizens, and buying foreign goods is the greatest shame of a citizen.

(3) The fashionable ladies and young ladies cannot find any imported goods on their bodies, in their houses, or in their stomachs.

(4) Knowledgeable women should use their time for meetings and socializing in factories to educate female workers and guide female workers to improve their lives.

。

(5) Women of the bourgeoisie should save their decoration fees and entertainment fees and invest in domestic goods factories.

(6) By the end of the year, the import surplus figures in the customs report will be reduced by several digits, and the import quantity of cosmetics will be almost zero.

(7) The newspapers publish news of the emergence, development, and expansion of small-scale family industrial organizations every day.

(8) The number of women waiting to be hired in Shanghai's employment agencies is gradually decreasing. Some are absorbed by domestic goods factories to take on jobs, and some return to the countryside to engage in their rural side businesses.

The above eight points are the achievements that I temporarily thought of for the Women's Domestic Goods Year. Maybe some people say that I take this Women's Domestic Goods Year too seriously. I also admit that I think that since it is stipulated as the Women's Domestic Goods Year, we should take it seriously and do some work. One of the biggest problems of our Chinese people is that we are not serious, so nothing is achieved. If everyone works seriously, I think the above eight points are not difficult to achieve. If everyone is unwilling to do it seriously, and still cannot show some achievements by the end of the year, I would like to suggest changing "Women's Domestic Goods Year" to "Women's Show-off Year", and ask the local collaboration association and several groups to retroactively recognize it, in order to match the name with the reality.

A Few Words to the Ladies

— Xuan Wan

Ladies! Young ladies! Please look at the following paragraphs.

I don't know from which year onwards, these blue-eyed children, dwarfs, they all took a fancy to us, opened our doors, and shipped their surplus goods into our country in large quantities. At the same time, several larger places and trading ports have become their dens for肆意搜刮. Buildings with more than a dozen floors. Buildings that are already towering high. They are foreign firms, foreign banks, and factories set up by foreign businessmen in China. They are all places to search and scrape our blood and sweat. In this way, year after year, tens of thousands of dollars flow from our pockets. Torrentially rolling to foreign lands.

Next, those foreign businessmen who set up factories in China, their capital is surplus, they have identified the things we need and lack, and they quickly find ways to manufacture and operate, and use our country's cheapest wages and raw materials, and rely on unequal treaties as护符, in this way, they have already taken the initial advantage.

Going a step further, they push these goods into our large companies and stores, relying on our many foreign goods salesmen to promote them. Let's not talk about anything else, let's just look at Nanjing Road, which is full of foreign atmosphere, how many large companies selling foreign goods are there? When the sun sets and the lights are lit, a group of fashionable girls, when their wives come out of the company, it can be said that everyone is holding their beloved foreign goods. We are promoting them hard, but you can always see them - the magnificent洋房 in the western suburbs of Shanghai. Which house is not a paradise for them to search our blood and sweat and enjoy it? Of course, we can also think that the cars that are running rampant on the road are all ridden by foreigners, and it is not only civilians who bow and smile at foreigners, but also politicians and important people.

Indeed, this is because we ourselves are not competitive, there is no need to say much. So, let's not talk about other years. In the Domestic Goods Year, a new record of an import surplus of 90 million yuan was revealed.

Our ladies, when you read the above words, you can be angry. Good! This year is the Women's Domestic Goods Year, and it is the time for you to contribute. Just hurry up and catch up. There is still nothing to worry about in the past. Ah! Get up!

How to Make the Women's National Products Year Work

— Dao Er

Last year was the National Products Year, but the customs deficit was still 410 million. Moreover, the domestic market was worse than in previous years, and people's purchasing power was exceptionally weak. However, so much money still flowed abroad to purchase foreign goods. If all 410 million had been used to buy domestic products, domestic factories would undoubtedly be more developed.

The reason why domestic goods cannot sell well now, as everyone knows, is largely due to the dumping of foreign goods. But we should also carefully study why foreign goods can make Chinese people willing to buy them. In general, people who are willing to buy foreign goods do not really want to send money to foreigners, nor do they necessarily hate and reject domestic goods. It is only because foreign goods are more beautiful and cheaper in style, while domestic goods have fewer designs and are more expensive, naturally attracting people to buy foreign goods instead of domestic goods when making purchases.

Some people say that buying foreign goods leads to money outflow, so it is better to buy domestic goods, even if the quality is worse and the price is higher, as the money remains in the country. Buying domestic goods is a national obligation and can even be said to be national morality. However, this is just a theory, and the reality is different. Because everyone's economic situation is different, if they can buy better things at a cheaper price, they will not care about domestic or foreign goods. Moreover, there is no law stipulating that buying foreign goods is a crime, so we can only persuade people to buy domestic goods, but not prohibit them from buying foreign goods. If domestic goods have good styles, good quality, and are plentiful, and the price is cheaper than foreign goods, then naturally there is no need to persuade people to buy them, and they will sell well naturally.

Therefore, I think that the Women's National Products Year's promotion of buying domestic products is still a passive way of promoting domestic products, rather than an active one. If we want to actively promote domestic products, we should find ways to urge domestic factories to work hard to improve their products, help them design and implement ways to reduce costs and lower prices as much as possible. On the other hand, we should also investigate all kinds of foreign and domestic goods, make a comparison table of their quality and prices, and give it to domestic factories to study how to make them as good as or even better than foreign goods. At the same time, in addition to reducing the cost of labor and materials, we should ask the government to reduce the tax rate on domestic goods, and domestic goods will naturally be welcomed by everyone. Generally speaking, the biggest disadvantage of domestic goods now is the lack of variety and the fact that their appearance is not as beautiful as foreign goods. This is the biggest reason. If we study this first, at least we can make the more affluent Chinese people adopt them first. There is already an example of this. Like the silk fabrics of the Mei Ya Silk Weaving Factory, they produce a lot, and the quality and style are better than foreign goods, and the price is low. Recently, their two-three spring style Luo Na silk has been bought by many Chinese women, and many foreigners also buy it. This shows that the first thing for a product to sell well is to have excellent quality. There is no need to repeatedly declare that it is a domestic product to attract others to buy it. If domestic goods do not improve quality and reduce prices, even if they are promoted as much as possible, or even if people give speeches to people in various countries saying that Chinese people must promote domestic goods and buy domestic goods, the effort will be twice the result.

This year is the Women's National Products Year. It would be best to ask those who are enthusiastic about the women's national products movement to first study the items used by women and how to improve or increase the styles of certain domestic products to a degree that suits women's preferences and uses. The second step is to find ways to reduce prices within the possible range. This is a very valuable and practical job!

Contributions from the Women's Circle

National Products and the Cultivation of a Sense of Duty

— Nie Zeng Jifen Nie Qijie, narrated

Today, the national affairs have declined to such an extent, and it is undeniable that the people lack a sense of duty. In general, officials have more intention of making money and less intention of fulfilling their duties, which I think is also a common feeling among ordinary people. Generally speaking, people today have a sense of suspicion towards the government and all public institutions. To go a step further, people's trust in each other is also weak, and they fear that the entrusted matters will not be handled faithfully. This is also a feeling that everyone has, which is also very sad. The progress of any progressive country does not only rely on perfect laws and regulations, but also on a large number of people with a spirit of responsibility to promote and benefit them to the fullest extent. Otherwise, even if there is a method of governance, it is equivalent to a mere formality. The so-called spirit of responsibility is the sense of duty. The people's sense of duty cannot be instilled suddenly, and there must be a method to cultivate it. Chinese doctrines since ancient times have emphasized this point everywhere. In short, it is to make society often have the concept of valuing righteousness over profit. In terms of division, each individual has their relative duties, which can be summarized by the five relationships, which is actually the responsibility to the entire group. For example, loyalty is for the ruler because he represents the entire group. Mencius's words on the righteousness of the ruler are the clearest: "A person who is cruel and tyrannical is called an ordinary man. I have heard of the execution of the tyrant Zhou, but I have not heard of the assassination of a ruler." Also, "The people are most important, and the ruler is least important." Therefore, loyalty to the ruler is loyalty to the group. Confucius said, "The ruler treats his ministers with courtesy, and the ministers serve the ruler with loyalty." Therefore, serving the ruler with loyalty has certain conditions, which must be within the scope of seeking the interests of the people. Promoting loyalty and righteousness is a good way to cultivate a sense of responsibility. For example, our society worships Guan Yu and Yue Fei. Those who read their books will naturally be inspired by the idea of defeating enemies and eliminating traitors. The north values chivalry and has thick customs, which is greatly influenced by this. Filial piety is for parents, which is also to correct the human weakness of valuing rights and neglecting obligations. Everything from pregnancy, nurturing, care, protection, education, and even marriage is done by the parents. When people grow up and become independent, they easily forget the past favors they have enjoyed, just like those who borrow money in society. At the time, they beg in every way, and when they get the money, they thank them a thousand times. But when it comes to repayment, even if they are rich, they often try to evade the debt, and often go to court. Another example is officials who only care about getting money and do not try to be competent, which is the same mentality. Ancient philosophers realized that humans have the same weaknesses, and believed that social order cannot be maintained by laws. It is necessary to cultivate everyone's sense of responsibility from an early age, so that they know that those who enjoy must repay. Therefore, they specially rewarded filial piety and punished unfilial piety. The state made it into law, and society formed clear opinions, and the effect was very obvious. There is an ancient saying, "Look for loyal ministers in the homes of filial sons." Looking at history, there has never been a filial person who was a corrupt official, and there has never been anyone who was filial to their parents and harmed the people. Why? They have a full sense of responsibility, despise rights and value obligations, so they can be incorruptible in the face of wealth and not avoid danger in the face of difficulty. Those who want to overthrow filial piety today have not thought deeply about the overall interests. Fidelity is for husband and wife, which is also an important matter for cultivating a sense of responsibility. Generally speaking, at the time of engagement, vows of eternal love are made, each with the expectation of growing old together. Are these sweet words intended to be tools for temporary love and seduction?

Or will there be a real intention to fulfill them? If one is determined to fulfill them and can actually practice their promises, then this is enough to be a manifestation of a sense of responsibility. Today, people often separate halfway and have other loves, mostly because they have met more handsome men and women, or because they are interested in their wealth and status. They disregard all vows and even abandon their children. This kind of behavior of losing a sense of responsibility is most common today. With such people, is it not difficult to devote themselves to the country and forget themselves in public matters? Recently, some people have advocated overthrowing chastity, glorifying it as the liberation of women. I think that overthrowing chastity is most unfavorable to women. Why? Although there are many theories of free love, in practice, men mostly take sexual desire and beauty as prerequisites, and women are easily blinded by emotions. There are very few who choose with reason. What women rely on is only beauty in a short period of ten years. After this period, they are easily disgusted by men. The old society was like this, and the new society is also like this. Moreover, because of pregnancy, women are prone to illness. When they are abandoned, their beauty has declined and it is difficult to marry again. Men are not like this. They age later, have stronger carnal desires, have no burden of pregnancy, and have stronger motivation to make a living, so they are often in a superior position. I have seen many women in society who are subjected to this oppression. In the past, the saying of chastity was indeed one-sided on the surface, but in fact, women received considerable protection. Even if men took concubines and openly abandoned their wives, there were not many in society. Women mostly guarded their chastity, and there were also many men who were loyal to their wives, driven by conscience. Since ancient times, enlightened people have never advocated encouraging young widows to remain chaste, and in the past, there was no legal compulsion to reward chastity. Only the spirit of perseverance was praised. Although the reward was only for women, the impact actually extended to the entire society. Now that this spirit has long disappeared, what is there left to overthrow? Moreover, the nature of our people has recently become increasingly frivolous and superficial, unable to foresee the future, and easily forgetful. The five-minute patriotic enthusiasm is laughed at by the world. Officials make solemn vows, but few can keep them. The weakness of the will and strength of the majority of people is undeniable. Today, if we want to save the situation, empty words will not be effective. We must start with improving eugenics and heredity, and cultivate a general group of young men and women with a serious and solemn style. There must be strong and steadfast parents, especially mothers, and then can healthy children be born. After repeated generations, there will be a majority of great-character people to clean up this broken and rotten situation. Educators and those responsible for guiding society, please do not forget this.

What ordinary people call loyalty, filial piety, integrity, and righteousness has long been regarded as pedantic and not worth mentioning. However, after careful analysis, it is so important to the cultivation of a sense of responsibility that the ancient people's promotion and role models were not pedantic. A few days ago, my child heard Mr. Huang Renzhi talk about recent events in Japan, saying that the Japanese people's spirit of responsibility is truly unmatched. How did they achieve this? It is because of the power of promotion and advancement. General Nogi won the war against the strong Russia, and the whole country respected him as a military god. When Emperor Meiji died, he killed himself to die for his ruler, and his wife also committed suicide at the high age of seventy to die for her husband. From the perspective of today's people, it seems meaningless, but its impact on the military and national training and social discipline is very large. Now there is Nogi Shrine in Tokyo. Those who pass by the door bow and pay their respects, making people associate sacrificing oneself for the country and sacrificing oneself for one's husband with winning the war against the strong Russia, and their sense of responsibility and willingness to sacrifice for the country will naturally arise. They can promote the old morality so that the spirit of patriotism is like that. Our people overthrow all rituals and teachings, and the current state of corruption is like this, which can not be deeply thought about? If the above can be implemented, not only can national products be promoted, but all national affairs can also be improved. I am willing to encourage and learn from you all to contribute to the one-in-ten-thousand.

What Constitutes a Perfectly Happy Family

— Yi Yi Guan Zhu

Huh! This publication is the "National Products Weekly," not a publication that studies women and families. Why would I raise such a question in this publication – what constitutes a perfectly happy family? I think: when you see this title, before reading the main text, you may have such doubts and such curiosity, right? In fact, to put it bluntly, there is no need to doubt, and there is nothing curious about it.

Because, among all living beings in the world, unless they are "monks" who embrace celibacy, who doesn't need a family? Especially a happy family, which is envied by everyone. Then, "what constitutes a perfectly happy family?" This question is very broad, and naturally, everyone urgently wants to know the answer. Moreover, in this "Women's National Products Year," it is even more something that everyone should understand. The question I am talking about now involves national products, so I will talk about it in this publication.

We know that the psychology of the general public regarding "happy families" can be summarized in one word: "happiness." However, I feel that in this day and age, a family that is simply "happy" cannot be said to be a "perfectly happy family," but can only be said to be a "nine-tenths happy family." There is still "one-tenth of happiness" that you should understand, which is to adopt "national products" for everything, whether it is clothing, food, or daily necessities. If you can't find even a little bit of "foreign goods" in your home, then your family is a "perfectly happy family"! Otherwise, it is "a fly in the ointment"! How can you talk about "perfect happiness"?
